    <DIV class="WordSection1 node-law">
 

 
<P class="shorttitle">Human Rights Code</P>
 
<P class="chapter">R.S.O. 1990, CHAPTER H.19</P>
 
<P class="ConsolidationPeriod"><B>Consolidation Period: </B>From May 18, 2023 to the <U><U>e-Laws currency date</U></U>.</P>
 
<P class="comment">Last amendment: 2023, c. 5, Sched. 2, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="10" href="#sec10_smooth">s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 

 
<P class="MsoNormal">  </P>
 
<P class="headnote">Preamble</P>
 
<P class="preamble"><A name="BK0"></A>Whereas recognition of the inherent dignity and the equal and inalienable rights of all members of the human family is the foundation of freedom, justice and peace in the world and is in accord with the Universal Declaration of Human Rights as proclaimed by the United Nations;</P>
 
<P class="preamble">And Whereas it is public policy in Ontario to recognize the dignity and worth of every person and to provide for equal rights and opportunities without discrimination that is contrary to law, and having as its aim the creation of a climate of understanding and mutual respect for the dignity and worth of each person so that each person feels a part of the community and able to contribute fully to the development and well-being of the community and the Province;</P>
 
<P class="preamble">And Whereas these principles have been confirmed in Ontario by a number of enactments of the Legislature and it is desirable to revise and extend the protection of human rights in Ontario;</P>
 
<P class="preamble">Therefore, Her Majesty, by and with the advice and consent of the Legislative Assembly of the Province of Ontario, enacts as follows:</P>
 
<A name="PART_I_FREEDOM_FROM_DISCRIMINATION_1632"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK1"></A>PART I <BR>  FREEDOM FROM DISCRIMINATION</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Services</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="577" data-noteup-count-display="577"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="1" data-viibes-start="0"><A name="BK2"></A><B><a name="sec1" id="sec1"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="1" subsection="null" alinea="null">1</SPAN> </B>Every person has a right to equal treatment with respect to services, goods and facilities, without discrimination because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, marital status, family status or disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 1; 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (1); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 1</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Accommodation</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="2" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec2" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=2"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="2" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="200" data-noteup-count-display="200"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="2" data-viibes-start="1" data-viibes-end="0"><A name="BK3"></A><B><a name="sec2subsec1" id="sec2subsec1"></A><a name="sec2" id="sec2"></A>2 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="2" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Every person has a right to equal treatment with respect to the occupancy of accommodation, without discrimination because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, marital status, family status, disability or the receipt of public assistance.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 2 (1); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (2)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 2 (1)</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec2subsec2" id="sec2subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Harassment in accommodation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="2" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Every person who occupies accommodation has a right to freedom from harassment by the landlord or agent of the landlord or by an occupant of the same building because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, marital status, family status, disability or the receipt of public assistance.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 2 (2); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (3); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (3)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 2 (2)</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Contracts</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="3" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec3" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=3"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="3" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="77" data-noteup-count-display="77"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="3" data-viibes-start="2" data-viibes-end="1"><A name="BK4"></A><B><a name="sec3" id="sec3"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="3" subsection="null" alinea="null">3</SPAN> </B>Every person having legal capacity has a right to contract on equal terms without discrimination because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, marital status, family status or disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 3; 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (4); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (4)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 3</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Accommodation of person under eighteen</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="4" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec4" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=4"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="4" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="72" data-noteup-count-display="72"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="4" data-viibes-start="3" data-viibes-end="2"><A name="BK5"></A><B><a name="sec4subsec1" id="sec4subsec1"></A><a name="sec4" id="sec4"></A>4 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="4" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Every sixteen or seventeen year old person who has withdrawn from parental control has a right to equal treatment with respect to occupancy of and contracting for accommodation without discrimination because the person is less than eighteen years old.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 4 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec4subsec2" id="sec4subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Idem</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="4" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> A contract for accommodation entered into by a sixteen or seventeen year old person who has withdrawn from parental control is enforceable against that person as if the person were eighteen years old.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 4 (2).</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Employment</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="5" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec5" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=5"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="5" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1070" data-noteup-count-display="1.1k"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="5" data-viibes-start="4" data-viibes-end="3"><A name="BK6"></A><B><a name="sec5subsec1" id="sec5subsec1"></A><a name="sec5" id="sec5"></A>5 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="5" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Every person has a right to equal treatment with respect to employment without discrimination because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, record of offences, marital status, family status or disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 5 (1); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (5); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (5)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 4 (1)</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec5subsec2" id="sec5subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Harassment in employment</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="5" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Every person who is an employee has a right to freedom from harassment in the workplace by the employer or agent of the employer or by another employee because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, record of offences, marital status, family status or disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 5 (2); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (6); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (6)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 4 (2)</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Vocational associations</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="6" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec6" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=6"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="6" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="98" data-noteup-count-display="98"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="6" data-viibes-start="5" data-viibes-end="4"><A name="BK7"></A><B><a name="sec6" id="sec6"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="6" subsection="null" alinea="null">6</SPAN> </B>Every person has a right to equal treatment with respect to membership in any trade union, trade or occupational association or self-governing profession without discrimination because of race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, citizenship, creed, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, gender expression, age, marital status, family status or disability. R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 6; 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (7); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (7)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Sexual harassment</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Harassment because of sex in accommodation</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="7" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec7" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=7"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="7" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="181" data-noteup-count-display="181"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="7" data-viibes-start="6" data-viibes-end="5"><A name="BK8"></A><B><a name="sec7subsec1" id="sec7subsec1"></A><a name="sec7" id="sec7"></A>7 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="7" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Every person who occupies accommodation has a right to freedom from harassment because of sex, sexual orientation, gender identity or gender expression by the landlord or agent of the landlord or by an occupant of the same building.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 7 (1); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 6 (1)</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec7subsec2" id="sec7subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Harassment because of sex in workplaces</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="7" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Every person who is an employee has a right to freedom from harassment in the workplace because of sex, sexual orientation, gender identity or gender expression by his or her employer or agent of the employer or by another employee.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 7 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96856-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2012-c-7/latest/so-2012-c-7.html">2012, c. 7, s. 6 (2)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec7subsec3" id="sec7subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Sexual solicitation by a person in position to confer benefit, etc.</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="7" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Every person has a right to be free from,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  a sexual solicitation or advance made by a person in a position to confer, grant or deny a benefit or advancement to the person where the person making the solicitation or advance knows or ought reasonably to know that it is unwelcome; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  a reprisal or a threat of reprisal for the rejection of a sexual solicitation or advance where the reprisal is made or threatened by a person in a position to confer, grant or deny a benefit or advancement to the person.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 7 (3).</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Reprisals</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="8" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec8" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=8"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="8" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="695" data-noteup-count-display="695"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="8" data-viibes-start="7" data-viibes-end="6"><A name="BK9"></A><B><a name="sec8" id="sec8"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="8" subsection="null" alinea="null">8</SPAN> </B>Every person has a right to claim and enforce his or her rights under this Act, to institute and participate in proceedings under this Act and to refuse to infringe a right of another person under this Act, without reprisal or threat of reprisal for so doing.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 8.</P></div>
 
<P class="headnote">Infringement prohibited</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="9" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec9" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=9"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="9" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="380" data-noteup-count-display="380"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="9" data-viibes-start="8" data-viibes-end="7"><A name="BK10"></A><B><a name="sec9" id="sec9"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="9" subsection="null" alinea="null">9</SPAN> </B>No person shall infringe or do, directly or indirectly, anything that infringes a right under this Part.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 9.</P></div>
 
<A name="PART_II_INTERPRETATION_AND_APPLICATION_8501"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK11"></A>PART II <BR>  INTERPRETATION AND APPLICATION</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Definitions re: Parts I and II</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="10" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec10" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=10"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="10" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="602" data-noteup-count-display="602"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="10" data-viibes-start="9" data-viibes-end="8"><A name="BK12"></A><B><a name="sec10subsec1" id="sec10subsec1"></A><a name="sec10" id="sec10"></A>10 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="10" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> In Part I and in this Part,</P></div>
 
<P class="definition">“age” means an age that is 18 years or more; (“âge”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“disability” means,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  any degree of physical disability, infirmity, malformation or disfigurement that is caused by bodily injury, birth defect or illness and, without limiting the generality of the foregoing, includes diabetes mellitus, epilepsy, a brain injury, any degree of paralysis, amputation, lack of physical co-ordination, blindness or visual impediment, deafness or hearing impediment, muteness or speech impediment, or physical reliance on a guide dog or other animal or on a wheelchair or other remedial appliance or device,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  a condition of mental impairment or a developmental disability,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  a learning disability, or a dysfunction in one or more of the processes involved in understanding or using symbols or spoken language,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  a mental disorder, or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  an injury or disability for which benefits were claimed or received under the insurance plan established under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="635-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-1997-c-16-sch-a/latest/so-1997-c-16-sch-a.html">Workplace Safety and Insurance Act, 1997</A></I>; (“handicap”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“equal” means subject to all requirements, qualifications and considerations that are not a prohibited ground of discrimination; (“égal”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“family status” means the status of being in a parent and child relationship; (“état familial”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“group insurance” means insurance whereby the lives or well-being or the lives and well-being of a number of persons are insured severally under a single contract between an insurer and an association or an employer or other person; (“assurance-groupe”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“harassment” means engaging in a course of vexatious comment or conduct that is known or ought reasonably to be known to be unwelcome; (“harcèlement”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“marital status” means the status of being married, single, widowed, divorced or separated and includes the status of living with a person in a conjugal relationship outside marriage; (“état matrimonial”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“record of offences” means a conviction for,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  an offence in respect of which a pardon has been granted under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="12793-current-1" href="/en/ca/laws/stat/rsc-1985-c-c-47/latest/rsc-1985-c-c-47.html">Criminal Records Act</A></I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="12793-current-1" href="/en/ca/laws/stat/rsc-1985-c-c-47/latest/rsc-1985-c-c-47.html"> (Canada)</A> and has not been revoked, or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  an offence in respect of any provincial enactment; (“casier judiciaire”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“services” does not include a levy, fee, tax or periodic payment imposed by law; (“services”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“spouse” means the person to whom a person is married or with whom the person is living in a conjugal relationship outside marriage. (“conjoint”)  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 10 (1); 1993, c. 27, Sched.; 1997, c. 16, s. 8; 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (8); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96560-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-13/latest/so-2001-c-13.html">2001, c. 13, s. 19</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27</A> (2, 3); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32</A> (8-10); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (1)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec10subsec2" id="sec10subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Pregnancy</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="10" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The right to equal treatment without discrimination because of sex includes the right to equal treatment without discrimination because a woman is or may become pregnant.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 10 (2).</P>
 
<a name="sec10subsec3" id="sec10subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Past and presumed disabilities</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="10" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The right to equal treatment without discrimination because of disability includes the right to equal treatment without discrimination because a person has or has had a disability or is believed to have or to have had a disability.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (4)</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Constructive discrimination</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="11" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec11" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=11"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="11" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="386" data-noteup-count-display="386"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="11" data-viibes-start="10" data-viibes-end="9"><A name="BK13"></A><B><a name="sec11subsec1" id="sec11subsec1"></A><a name="sec11" id="sec11"></A>11 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="11" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> A right of a person under Part I is infringed where a requirement, qualification or factor exists that is not discrimination on a prohibited ground but that results in the exclusion, restriction or preference of a group of persons who are identified by a prohibited ground of discrimination and of whom the person is a member, except where,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  the requirement, qualification or factor is reasonable and <I>bona fide</I> in the circumstances; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  it is declared in this Act, other than in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="17" href="#sec17_smooth">section 17</A>, that to discriminate because of such ground is not an infringement of a right.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 11 (1).</P>
 
<a name="sec11subsec2" id="sec11subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Idem</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="11" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Tribunal or a court shall not find that a requirement, qualification or factor is reasonable and <I>bona fide</I> in the circumstances unless it is satisfied that the needs of the group of which the person is a member cannot be accommodated without undue hardship on the person responsible for accommodating those needs, considering the cost, outside sources of funding, if any, and health and safety requirements, if any.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 11 (2); 1994, c. 27, s. 65 (1); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96598-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html">2002, c. 18</A>, Sched. C, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" ss="1" href="#sec2subsec1_smooth">s. 2 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96804-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2009-c-33/latest/so-2009-c-33.html">2009, c. 33</A>, Sched. 2, s. 35 (1).</P>
 
<a name="sec11subsec3" id="sec11subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Idem</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="11" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Tribunal or a court shall consider any standards prescribed by the regulations for assessing what is undue hardship.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 11 (3); 1994, c. 27, s. 65 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96598-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html">2002, c. 18</A>, Sched. C, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" ss="2" href="#sec2subsec2_smooth">s. 2 (2)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96804-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2009-c-33/latest/so-2009-c-33.html">2009, c. 33</A>, Sched. 2, s. 35 (2).</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Discrimination because of association</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="12" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec12" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=12"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="12" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="46" data-noteup-count-display="46"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="12" data-viibes-start="11" data-viibes-end="10"><A name="BK14"></A><B><a name="sec12" id="sec12"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="12" subsection="null" alinea="null">12</SPAN> </B>A right under Part I is infringed where the discrimination is because of relationship, association or dealings with a person or persons identified by a prohibited ground of discrimination.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 12.</P></div>
 
<P class="headnote">Announced intention to discriminate</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="13" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec13" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=13"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="13" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="70" data-noteup-count-display="70"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="13" data-viibes-start="12" data-viibes-end="11"><A name="BK15"></A><B><a name="sec13subsec1" id="sec13subsec1"></A><a name="sec13" id="sec13"></A>13 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="13" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> A right under Part I is infringed by a person who publishes or displays before the public or causes the publication or display before the public of any notice, sign, symbol, emblem, or other similar representation that indicates the intention of the person to infringe a right under Part I or that is intended by the person to incite the infringement of a right under Part I.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 13 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec13subsec2" id="sec13subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Opinion</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="13" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Subsection (1) shall not interfere with freedom of expression of opinion.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 13 (2).</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Special programs</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="14" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec14" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=14"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="14" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="65" data-noteup-count-display="65"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="14" data-viibes-start="13" data-viibes-end="12"><A name="BK16"></A><B><a name="sec14subsec1" id="sec14subsec1"></A><a name="sec14" id="sec14"></A>14 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="14" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> A right under Part I is not infringed by the implementation of a special program designed to relieve hardship or economic disadvantage or to assist disadvantaged persons or groups to achieve or attempt to achieve equal opportunity or that is likely to contribute to the elimination of the infringement of rights under Part I.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 14 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec14subsec2" id="sec14subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Application to Commission</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> A person may apply to the Commission for a designation of a program as a special program for the purposes of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec3" id="sec14subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Designation by Commission</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Upon receipt of an application, the Commission may, </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  designate the program as a special program if, in its opinion, the program meets the requirements of subsection (1); or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  designate the program as a special program on the condition that the program make such modifications as are specified in the designation in order to meet the requirements of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec4" id="sec14subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Inquiries initiated by Commission</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The Commission may, on its own initiative, inquire into one or more programs to determine whether the programs are special programs for the purposes of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec5" id="sec14subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">End of inquiry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> At the conclusion of an inquiry under subsection (4), the Commission may designate as a special program any of the programs under inquiry if, in its opinion, the programs meet the requirements of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec6" id="sec14subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Expiry of designation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> A designation under subsection (3) or (5) expires five years after the day it is issued or at such earlier time as may be specified by the Commission.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec7" id="sec14subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Renewal of designation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> If an application for renewal of a designation of a program as a special program is made to the Commission before its expiry under subsection (6), the Commission may,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  renew the designation if, in its opinion, the program continues to meet the requirements of subsection (1); or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  renew the designation on the condition that the program make such modifications as are specified in the designation in order to meet the requirements of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec8" id="sec14subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Effect of designation, etc.</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> In a proceeding, </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  evidence that a program has been designated as a special program under this section is proof, in the absence of evidence to the contrary, that the program is a special program for the purposes of subsection (1); and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  evidence that the Commission has considered and refused to designate a program as a special program under this section is proof, in the absence of evidence to the contrary, that the program is not a special program for the purposes of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec9" id="sec14subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Crown programs</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> Subsections (2) to (8) do not apply to a program implemented by the Crown or an agency of the Crown.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec14subsec10" id="sec14subsec10"></A><P class="headnote">Tribunal finding</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="14" subsection="10" alinea="null">(10)</SPAN> For the purposes of a proceeding before the Tribunal, the Tribunal may make a finding that a program meets the requirements of a special program under subsection (1), even though the program has not been designated as a special program by the Commission under this section, subject to clause (8) (b).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 1</A>.</P>
 

 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="14.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec14.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=14.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="14.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1" data-noteup-count-display="1"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="14.1" data-viibes-start="14" data-viibes-end="13"><B><a name="sec14.1" id="sec14_1"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="14.1" subsection="null" alinea="null">14.1</SPAN></B> Repealed:  1995, c. 4, s. 3 (1).</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Age sixty-five or over</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="15" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec15" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=15"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="15" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="24" data-noteup-count-display="24"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="15" data-viibes-start="15" data-viibes-end="14"><A name="BK17"></A><B><a name="sec15" id="sec15"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="15" subsection="null" alinea="null">15</SPAN> </B>A right under Part I to non-discrimination because of age is not infringed where an age of sixty-five years or over is a requirement, qualification or consideration for preferential treatment.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 15.</P></div>
 
<P class="headnote">Canadian Citizenship</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="16" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec16" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=16"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="16" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="24" data-noteup-count-display="24"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="16" data-viibes-start="16" data-viibes-end="15"><A name="BK18"></A><B><a name="sec16subsec1" id="sec16subsec1"></A><a name="sec16" id="sec16"></A>16 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="16" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> A right under Part I to non-discrimination because of citizenship is not infringed where Canadian citizenship is a requirement, qualification or consideration imposed or authorized by law.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 16 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec16subsec2" id="sec16subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Idem</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="16" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> A right under Part I to non-discrimination because of citizenship is not infringed where Canadian citizenship or lawful admission to Canada for permanent residence is a requirement, qualification or consideration adopted for the purpose of fostering and developing participation in cultural, educational, trade union or athletic activities by Canadian citizens or persons lawfully admitted to Canada for permanent residence.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 16 (2).</P>
 
<a name="sec16subsec3" id="sec16subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Idem</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="16" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> A right under Part I to non-discrimination because of citizenship is not infringed where Canadian citizenship or domicile in Canada with the intention to obtain Canadian citizenship is a requirement, qualification or consideration adopted by an organization or enterprise for the holder of chief or senior executive positions.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 16 (3).</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Disability</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="17" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec17" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=17"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="17" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="321" data-noteup-count-display="321"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="17" data-viibes-start="17" data-viibes-end="16"><A name="BK19"></A><B><a name="sec17subsec1" id="sec17subsec1"></A><a name="sec17" id="sec17"></A>17 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="17" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> A right of a person under this Act is not infringed for the reason only that the person is incapable of performing or fulfilling the essential duties or requirements attending the exercise of the right because of disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 17 (1); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (5)</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec17subsec2" id="sec17subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Accommodation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="17" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> No tribunal or court shall find a person incapable unless it is satisfied that the needs of the person cannot be accommodated without undue hardship on the person responsible for accommodating those needs, considering the cost, outside sources of funding, if any, and health and safety requirements, if any.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 17 (2); 1994, c. 27, s. 65 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96598-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html">2002, c. 18</A>, Sched. C, <SPAN class="reflex2-link" link-count="1" link1="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html#sec3subsec1" title1="Government Efficiency Act, 2002, SO 2002, c 18 (Ontario)" concatenated-id="96598" s="3" ss="1" data-link-type="weak">s. 3 (1)</SPAN>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 2 (1)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec17subsec3" id="sec17subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Determining if undue hardship</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="17" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> In determining for the purposes of subsection (2) whether there would be undue hardship, a tribunal or court shall consider any standards prescribed by the regulations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 2 (2)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec17subsec4" id="sec17subsec4"></A><P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="17" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> Repealed:  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 2 (3)</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Special interest organizations</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="18" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec18" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=18"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="18" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="16" data-noteup-count-display="16"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="18" data-viibes-start="18" data-viibes-end="17"><A name="BK20"></A><B><a name="sec18" id="sec18"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="18" subsection="null" alinea="null">18</SPAN> </B>The rights under Part I to equal treatment with respect to services and facilities, with or without accommodation, are not infringed where membership or participation in a religious, philanthropic, educational, fraternal or social institution or organization that is primarily engaged in serving the interests of persons identified by a prohibited ground of discrimination is restricted to persons who are similarly identified.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 18; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96712-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-19/latest/so-2006-c-19.html">2006, c. 19</A>, Sched. B, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="10" href="#sec10_smooth">s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Solemnization of marriage by religious officials</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="18.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec18.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=18.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="18.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="4" data-noteup-count-display="4"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="18.1" data-viibes-start="19" data-viibes-end="18"><A name="BK21"></A><B><a name="sec18.1subsec1" id="sec18_1subsec1"></A><a name="sec18.1" id="sec18_1"></A>18.1</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="18.1" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The rights under Part I to equal treatment with respect to services and facilities are not infringed where a person registered under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="282-current-1" s="20.1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-m3/latest/rso-1990-c-m3.html#sec20.1_smooth">section 20.1</A> or <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="282-current-1" s="20.3" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-m3/latest/rso-1990-c-m3.html#sec20.3_smooth">section 20.3</A> of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="282-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-m3/latest/rso-1990-c-m3.html">Marriage Act</A></I> refuses to solemnize a marriage, to allow a sacred place to be used for solemnizing a marriage or for an event related to the solemnization of a marriage, or to otherwise assist in the solemnization of a marriage, if to solemnize the marriage, allow the sacred place to be used or otherwise assist<B> </B>would be contrary to,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  the person’s religious beliefs; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  the doctrines, rites, usages or customs of the religious body to which the person belongs.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (11)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97053-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2020-c-11/latest/so-2020-c-11.html">2020, c. 11</A>, Sched. 17, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="6" href="#sec6_smooth">s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec18.1subsec2" id="sec18_1subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="18.1" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Nothing in subsection (1) limits the application of <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="18" href="#sec18_smooth">section 18</A>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (11)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec18.1subsec3" id="sec18_1subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Definition</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="18.1" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> In this section,</P>
 
<P class="definition">“sacred place” includes a place of worship and any ancillary or accessory facilities.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (11)</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Separate school rights preserved</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="19" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec19" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=19"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="19" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="35" data-noteup-count-display="35"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="19" data-viibes-start="20" data-viibes-end="19"><A name="BK22"></A><B><a name="sec19subsec1" id="sec19subsec1"></A><a name="sec19" id="sec19"></A>19 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="19" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> This Act shall not be construed to adversely affect any right or privilege respecting separate schools enjoyed by separate school boards or their supporters under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="36027-current-1" href="/en/ca/laws/stat/30---31-vict-c-3/latest/30---31-vict-c-3.html">Constitution Act, 1867</A></I> and the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="130-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-e2/latest/rso-1990-c-e2.html">Education Act</A></I>.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 19 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec19subsec2" id="sec19subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Duties of teachers</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="19" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> This Act does not apply to affect the application of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="130-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-e2/latest/rso-1990-c-e2.html">Education Act</A></I> with respect to the duties of teachers.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 19 (2).</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Restriction of facilities by sex</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="20" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec20" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=20"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="20" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="21" data-noteup-count-display="21"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="20" data-viibes-start="21" data-viibes-end="20"><A name="BK23"></A><B><a name="sec20subsec1" id="sec20subsec1"></A><a name="sec20" id="sec20"></A>20 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="20" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="1" href="#sec1_smooth">section 1</A> to equal treatment with respect to services and facilities without discrimination because of sex is not infringed where the use of the services or facilities is restricted to persons of the same sex on the ground of public decency.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 20 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec20subsec2" id="sec20subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Minimum drinking age</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="20" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="1" href="#sec1_smooth">section 1</A> to equal treatment with respect to services, goods and facilities without discrimination because of age is not infringed by the provisions of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="60196-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2019-c-15-sch-22/latest/so-2019-c-15-sch-22.html">Liquor Licence and Control Act, 2019</A></I> and the regulations under it relating to providing for and enforcing a minimum drinking age of nineteen years.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 20 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97039-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2019-c-15/latest/so-2019-c-15.html">2019, c. 15</A>, Sched. 22, <SPAN class="reflex2-link" link-count="1" link1="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2019-c-15/latest/so-2019-c-15.html#sec95" title1="Plan to Build Ontario Together Act, 2019, SO 2019, c 15 (Ontario)" concatenated-id="97039" s="95" data-link-type="weak">s. 95</SPAN>.</P>
 
<a name="sec20subsec3" id="sec20subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Recreational clubs</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="20" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="1" href="#sec1_smooth">section 1</A> to equal treatment with respect to services and facilities is not infringed where a recreational club restricts or qualifies access to its services or facilities or gives preferences with respect to membership dues and other fees because of age, sex, marital status or family status.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 20 (3); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (9); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (12)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec20subsec4" id="sec20subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Young persons and certain products</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="20" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="1" href="#sec1_smooth">section 1</A> to equal treatment with respect to goods without discrimination because of age is not infringed by the provisions of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="43849-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2017-c-26-sch-3/latest/so-2017-c-26-sch-3.html">Smoke-Free Ontario Act, 2017</A></I>
and the regulations under it relating to selling or supplying anything to which that Act applies to persons who are, or who appear to be, under the age of 19 years or 25 years, as the case may be. <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96998-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-26/latest/so-2017-c-26.html">2017, c. 26</A>, Sched. 3, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="26" href="#sec26_smooth">s. 26</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec20subsec5" id="sec20subsec5"></A><P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="20" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> Repealed: <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96998-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-26/latest/so-2017-c-26.html">2017, c. 26</A>, Sched. 3, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="26" href="#sec26_smooth">s. 26</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Residential accommodation</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Shared accommodation</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="21" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec21" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=21"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="21" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="30" data-noteup-count-display="30"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="21" data-viibes-start="22" data-viibes-end="21"><A name="BK24"></A><B><a name="sec21subsec1" id="sec21subsec1"></A><a name="sec21" id="sec21"></A>21 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="21" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" href="#sec2_smooth">section 2</A> to equal treatment with respect to the occupancy of residential accommodation without discrimination is not infringed by discrimination where the residential accommodation is in a dwelling in which the owner or his or her family reside if the occupant or occupants of the residential accommodation are required to share a bathroom or kitchen facility with the owner or family of the owner.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 21 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec21subsec2" id="sec21subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Restrictions on accommodation, sex</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="21" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" href="#sec2_smooth">section 2</A> to equal treatment with respect to the occupancy of residential accommodation without discrimination because of sex is not infringed by discrimination on that ground where the occupancy of all the residential accommodation in the building, other than the accommodation, if any, of the owner or family of the owner, is restricted to persons who are of the same sex.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 21 (2).</P>
 
<a name="sec21subsec3" id="sec21subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Prescribing business practices</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="21" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" href="#sec2_smooth">section 2</A> to equal treatment with respect to the occupancy of residential accommodation without discrimination is not infringed if a landlord uses in the manner prescribed under this Act income information, credit checks, credit references, rental history, guarantees or other similar business practices which are prescribed in the regulations made under this Act in selecting prospective tenants.  1997, c. 24, s. 212 (1).</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Restrictions for insurance contracts, etc.</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="22" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec22" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=22"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="22" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="26" data-noteup-count-display="26"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="22" data-viibes-start="23" data-viibes-end="22"><A name="BK25"></A><B><a name="sec22" id="sec22"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="22" subsection="null" alinea="null">22</SPAN> </B>The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="1" href="#sec1_smooth">sections 1</A> and <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="3" href="#sec3_smooth">3</A> to equal treatment with respect to services and to contract on equal terms, without discrimination because of age, sex, marital status, family status or disability, is not infringed where a contract of automobile, life, accident or sickness or disability insurance or a contract of group insurance between an insurer and an association or person other than an employer, or a life annuity, differentiates or makes a distinction, exclusion or preference on reasonable and <I>bona fide</I> grounds because of age, sex, marital status, family status or disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 22; 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (10); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (5)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (13)</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Employment</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="23" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec23" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=23"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="23" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="43" data-noteup-count-display="43"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="23" data-viibes-start="24" data-viibes-end="23"><A name="BK26"></A><B><a name="sec23subsec1" id="sec23subsec1"></A><a name="sec23" id="sec23"></A>23 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="23" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment is infringed where an invitation to apply for employment or an advertisement in connection with employment is published or displayed that directly or indirectly classifies or indicates qualifications by a prohibited ground of discrimination.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 23 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec23subsec2" id="sec23subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Application for employment</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="23" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment is infringed where a form of application for employment is used or a written or oral inquiry is made of an applicant that directly or indirectly classifies or indicates qualifications by a prohibited ground of discrimination.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 23 (2).</P>
 
<a name="sec23subsec3" id="sec23subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Questions at interview</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="23" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Nothing in subsection (2) precludes the asking of questions at a personal employment interview concerning a prohibited ground of discrimination where discrimination on such ground is permitted under this Act.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 23 (3).</P>
 
<a name="sec23subsec4" id="sec23subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Employment agencies</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="23" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment is infringed where an employment agency discriminates against a person because of a prohibited ground of discrimination in receiving, classifying, disposing of or otherwise acting upon applications for its services or in referring an applicant or applicants to an employer or agent of an employer.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 23 (4).</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Special employment</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="24" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec24" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=24"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="24" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="95" data-noteup-count-display="95"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="24" data-viibes-start="25" data-viibes-end="24"><A name="BK27"></A><B><a name="sec24subsec1" id="sec24subsec1"></A><a name="sec24" id="sec24"></A>24 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="24" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment is not infringed where,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  a religious, philanthropic, educational, fraternal or social institution or organization that is primarily engaged in serving the interests of persons identified by their race, ancestry, place of origin, colour, ethnic origin, creed, sex, age, marital status or disability employs only, or gives preference in employment to, persons similarly identified if the qualification is a reasonable and <I>bona fide</I>
qualification because of the nature of the employment;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  the discrimination in employment is for reasons of age, sex, record of offences or marital status if the age, sex, record of offences or marital status of the applicant is a reasonable and <I>bona fide</I> qualification because of the nature of the employment;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  an individual person refuses to employ another for reasons of any prohibited ground of discrimination in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A>, where the primary duty of the employment is attending to the medical or personal needs of the person or of an ill child or an aged, infirm or ill spouse or other relative of the person;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  an employer grants or withholds employment or advancement in employment to a person who is the spouse, child or parent of the employer or an employee;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  a judge is required to retire or cease to continue in office on reaching a specified age under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="89-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-c43/latest/rso-1990-c-c43.html">Courts of Justice Act</A></I>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (f)  an associate judge is required to retire on reaching a specified age under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="89-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-c43/latest/rso-1990-c-c43.html">Courts of Justice Act</A></I>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (g)  the term of reappointment of an associate judge expires on the associate judge reaching a specified age under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="89-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-c43/latest/rso-1990-c-c43.html">Courts of Justice Act</A></I>; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (h)  a justice of the peace is required to retire on reaching a specified age under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="231-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-j4/latest/rso-1990-c-j4.html">Justices of the Peace Act</A></I>.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 24 (1); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (11); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (5)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (14)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (2)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96958-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2016-c-23/latest/so-2016-c-23.html">2016, c. 23, s. 54</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97053-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2020-c-11/latest/so-2020-c-11.html">2020, c. 11</A>, Sched. 5, s. 16 (1); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97082-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2021-c-4/latest/so-2021-c-4.html">2021, c. 4</A>, Sched. 11, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="16" href="#sec16_smooth">s. 16</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97082-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2021-c-4/latest/so-2021-c-4.html">2021, c. 4</A>, Sched. 3, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="23" href="#sec23_smooth">s. 23</A> (1, 2).</P>
 
<a name="sec24subsec2" id="sec24subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Reasonable accommodation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="24" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> No tribunal or court shall find that a qualification under clause (1) (b) is reasonable and <I>bona fide</I> unless it is satisfied that the circumstances of the person cannot be accommodated without undue hardship on the person responsible for accommodating those circumstances considering the cost, outside sources of funding, if any, and health and safety requirements, if any.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 24 (2); 1994, c. 27, s. 65 (4); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96598-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html">2002, c. 18</A>, Sched. C, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="4" ss="1" href="#sec4subsec1_smooth">s. 4 (1)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 3 (1)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec24subsec3" id="sec24subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Determining if undue hardship</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="24" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> In determining for the purposes of subsection (2) whether there would be undue hardship, a tribunal or court shall consider any standards prescribed by the regulations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 3 (2)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec24subsec4" id="sec24subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="24" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="24" ss="1" href="#sec24subsec1_smooth">Clauses 24 (1)</A> (e), (f), (g) and (h) shall not be interpreted to suggest that a judge, associate judge or justice of the peace is an employee for the purposes of this Act or any other Act or law.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (3)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97053-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2020-c-11/latest/so-2020-c-11.html">2020, c. 11</A>, Sched. 5, s. 16 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97082-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2021-c-4/latest/so-2021-c-4.html">2021, c. 4</A>, Sched. 3, s. 23 (3).</P>
 

 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="24.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec24.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=24.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="24.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="24.1" data-viibes-start="26" data-viibes-end="25"><B><a name="sec24.1" id="sec24_1"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="24.1" subsection="null" alinea="null">24.1</SPAN></B> Repealed: 1995, c. 4, s. 3 (2).</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Employee benefit and pension plans</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="25" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec25" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=25"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="25" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="50" data-noteup-count-display="50"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="25" data-viibes-start="27" data-viibes-end="26"><A name="BK28"></A><B><a name="sec25subsec1" id="sec25subsec1"></A><a name="sec25" id="sec25"></A>25 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="25" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment is infringed where employment is denied or made conditional because a term or condition of employment requires enrolment in an employee benefit, pension or superannuation plan or fund or a contract of group insurance between an insurer and an employer, that makes a distinction, preference or exclusion on a prohibited ground of discrimination.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 25 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec25subsec2" id="sec25subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="25" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment without discrimination because of sex, marital status or family status is not infringed by an employee superannuation or pension plan or fund or a contract of group insurance between an insurer and an employer that complies with the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="713-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2000-c-41/latest/so-2000-c-41.html">Employment Standards Act, 2000</A> </I>and the regulations thereunder.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 25 (2); 1999, c. 6, s. 28 (12); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96663-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-5/latest/so-2005-c-5.html">2005, c. 5, s. 32 (15)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (4)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec25subsec2.1" id="sec25subsec2_1"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="25" subsection="2.1" alinea="null">(2.1)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment without discrimination because of age is not infringed by an employee benefit, pension, superannuation or group insurance plan or fund that complies with the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="713-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2000-c-41/latest/so-2000-c-41.html">Employment Standards Act, 2000</A></I> and the regulations thereunder.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (5)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec25subsec2.2" id="sec25subsec2_2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="25" subsection="2.2" alinea="null">(2.2)</SPAN> Subsection (2.1) applies whether or not a plan or fund is the subject of a contract of insurance between an insurer and an employer.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (5)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec25subsec2.3" id="sec25subsec2_3"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="25" subsection="2.3" alinea="null">(2.3)</SPAN> For greater certainty, subsections (2) and (2.1) apply whether or not “age”, “sex” or “marital status” in the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="713-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2000-c-41/latest/so-2000-c-41.html">Employment Standards Act, 2000</A></I> or the regulations under it have the same meaning as those terms have in this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96687-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2005-c-29/latest/so-2005-c-29.html">2005, c. 29, s. 1 (5)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec25subsec3" id="sec25subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="25" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> to equal treatment with respect to employment without discrimination because of disability is not infringed,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  where a reasonable and <I>bona fide</I>
distinction, exclusion or preference is made in an employee disability or life insurance plan or benefit because of a pre-existing disability that substantially increases the risk;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  where a reasonable and <I>bona fide</I> distinction, exclusion or preference is made on the ground of a pre-existing disability in respect of an employee-pay-all or participant-pay-all benefit in an employee benefit, pension or superannuation plan or fund or a contract of group insurance between an insurer and an employer or in respect of a plan, fund or policy that is offered by an employer to employees if they are fewer than twenty-five in number.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 25 (3); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (5)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec25subsec4" id="sec25subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Compensation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="25" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> An employer shall pay to an employee who is excluded because of a disability from an employee benefit, pension or superannuation plan or fund or a contract of group insurance between an insurer and the employer compensation equivalent to the contribution that the employer would make thereto on behalf of an employee who does not have a disability.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 25 (4); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96579-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2001-c-32/latest/so-2001-c-32.html">2001, c. 32, s. 27 (5)</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Discrimination in employment under government contracts</P>
