<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="26" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec26" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=26"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="26" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="11" data-noteup-count-display="11"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="26" data-viibes-start="28" data-viibes-end="27"><A name="BK29"></A><B><a name="sec26subsec1" id="sec26subsec1"></A><a name="sec26" id="sec26"></A>26 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="26" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> It shall be deemed to be a condition of every contract entered into by or on behalf of the Crown or any agency thereof and of every subcontract entered into in the performance thereof that no right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> will be infringed in the course of performing the contract.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 26 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec26subsec2" id="sec26subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Idem: government grants and loans</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="26" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> It shall be deemed to be a condition of every grant, contribution, loan or guarantee made by or on behalf of the Crown or any agency thereof that no right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> will be infringed in the course of carrying out the purposes for which the grant, contribution, loan or guarantee was made.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 26 (2).</P>
 
<a name="sec26subsec3" id="sec26subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Sanction</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="26" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Where an infringement of a right under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">section 5</A> is found by the Tribunal upon a complaint and constitutes a breach of a condition under this section, the breach of condition is sufficient grounds for cancellation of the contract, grant, contribution, loan or guarantee and refusal to enter into any further contract with or make any further grant, contribution, loan or guarantee to the same person.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 26 (3); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96598-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html">2002, c. 18</A>, Sched. C, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" href="#sec5_smooth">s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<A name="Part_III_The_ontario_human_rights_commission_39147"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK30"></A>Part III <BR>  The ontario human rights commission</P>
 
<P class="headnote">The Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="27" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec27" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=27"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="27" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="24" data-noteup-count-display="24"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="27" data-viibes-start="29" data-viibes-end="28"><A name="BK31"></A><B><a name="sec27subsec1" id="sec27subsec1"></A><a name="sec27" id="sec27"></A>27 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="27" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Ontario Human Rights Commission is continued under the name Ontario Human Rights Commission in English and Commission ontarienne des droits de la personne in French.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec27subsec2" id="sec27subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Composition</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Commission shall be composed of such persons as are appointed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec3" id="sec27subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Appointment</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Every person appointed to the Commission shall have knowledge, experience or training with respect to human rights law and issues.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec4" id="sec27subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Criteria</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> In the appointment of persons to the Commission under subsection (2), the importance of reflecting, in the composition of the Commission as a whole, the diversity of Ontario’s population shall be recognized.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec5" id="sec27subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Chief Commissioner</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council shall designate a member of the Commission as Chief Commissioner.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec6" id="sec27subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Powers and duties of Chief Commissioner</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> The Chief Commissioner shall direct the Commission and exercise the powers and perform the duties assigned to the Chief Commissioner by or under this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec7" id="sec27subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Term of office</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> The Chief Commissioner and other members of the Commission shall hold office for such term as may be specified by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec8" id="sec27subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Remuneration</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> The Chief Commissioner and other members of the Commission shall be paid such remuneration and allowance for expenses as are fixed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec9" id="sec27subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Employees</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> The Commission may appoint such employees as it considers necessary for the proper conduct of its affairs and the employees shall be appointed under Part III of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="825-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2006-c-35-sch-a/latest/so-2006-c-35-sch-a.html">Public Service of Ontario Act, 2006</A></I>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96728-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-35/latest/so-2006-c-35.html">2006, c. 35</A>, Sched. C, <SPAN class="reflex2-link" link-count="1" link1="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-35/latest/so-2006-c-35.html#sec132subsec5" title1="Public Service of Ontario Statute Law Amendment Act, 2006, SO 2006, c 35 (Ontario)" concatenated-id="96728" s="132" ss="5" data-link-type="weak">s. 132 (5)</SPAN>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec10" id="sec27subsec10"></A><P class="headnote">Evidence obtained in performance of duties</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="10" alinea="null">(10)</SPAN> A member of the Commission shall not be required to give testimony in a civil suit or any proceeding as to information obtained in the performance of duties under this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec11" id="sec27subsec11"></A><P class="headnote">Same, employees</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="11" alinea="null">(11)</SPAN> An employee of the Commission shall not be required to give testimony in a civil suit or any proceeding other than a proceeding under this Act as to information obtained in the performance of duties under this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec12" id="sec27subsec12"></A><P class="headnote">Delegation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="12" alinea="null">(12)</SPAN> The Chief Commissioner may in writing delegate any of his or her powers, duties or functions under this Act to any member of the Anti-Racism Secretariat, the Disability Rights Secretariat or an advisory group or to any other member of the Commission, subject to such conditions as the Chief Commissioner may set out in the delegation.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec27subsec13" id="sec27subsec13"></A><P class="headnote">Divisions</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="27" subsection="13" alinea="null">(13)</SPAN> The Commission may authorize any function of the Commission to be performed by a division of the Commission composed of at least three members of the Commission.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Acting Chief Commissioner</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="28" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec28" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=28"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="28" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="28" data-viibes-start="30" data-viibes-end="29"><A name="BK32"></A><B><a name="sec28subsec1" id="sec28subsec1"></A><a name="sec28" id="sec28"></A>28 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="28" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> If the Chief Commissioner dies, resigns or is unable or neglects to perform his or her duties, the Lieutenant Governor in Council may appoint an Acting Chief Commissioner to hold office for such period as may be specified in the appointment.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec28subsec2" id="sec28subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="28" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> An Acting Chief Commissioner shall perform the duties and have the powers of the Chief Commissioner and shall be paid such remuneration and allowance for expenses as are fixed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Functions of Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="29" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec29" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=29"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="29" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="13" data-noteup-count-display="13"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="29" data-viibes-start="31" data-viibes-end="30"><A name="BK33"></A><B><a name="sec29" id="sec29"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="29" subsection="null" alinea="null">29</SPAN> </B>The functions of the Commission are to promote and advance respect for human rights in Ontario, to protect human rights in Ontario and, recognizing that it is in the public interest to do so and that it is the Commission’s duty to protect the public interest, to identify and promote the elimination of discriminatory practices and, more specifically,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  to forward the policy that the dignity and worth of every person be recognized and that equal rights and opportunities be provided without discrimination that is contrary to law;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  to develop and conduct programs of public information and education to,</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (i)  promote awareness and understanding of, respect for and compliance with this Act, and</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (ii)  prevent and eliminate discriminatory practices that infringe rights under Part I;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  to undertake, direct and encourage research into discriminatory practices and to make recommendations designed to prevent and eliminate such discriminatory practices;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  to examine and review any statute or regulation, and any program or policy made by or under a statute, and make recommendations on any provision, program or policy that in its opinion is inconsistent with the intent of this Act;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  to initiate reviews and inquiries into incidents of tension or conflict, or conditions that lead or may lead to incidents of tension or conflict, in a community, institution, industry or sector of the economy, and to make recommendations, and encourage and co-ordinate plans, programs and activities, to reduce or prevent such incidents or sources of tension or conflict;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (f)  to promote, assist and encourage public, municipal or private agencies, organizations, groups or persons to engage in programs to alleviate tensions and conflicts based upon identification by a prohibited ground of discrimination;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (g)  to designate programs as special programs in accordance with <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="14" href="#sec14_smooth">section 14</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (h)  to approve policies under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="30" href="#sec30_smooth">section 30</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (i)  to make applications to the Tribunal under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth">section 35</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (j)  to report to the people of Ontario on the state of human rights in Ontario and on its affairs;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (k)  to perform the functions assigned to the Commission under this or any other Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Commission policies</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="30" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec30" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=30"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="30" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="5" data-noteup-count-display="5"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="30" data-viibes-start="32" data-viibes-end="31"><A name="BK34"></A><B><a name="sec30" id="sec30"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="30" subsection="null" alinea="null">30</SPAN> </B>The Commission may approve policies prepared and published by the Commission to provide guidance in the application of Parts I and II.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Inquiries</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="9" data-noteup-count-display="9"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31" data-viibes-start="33" data-viibes-end="32"><A name="BK35"></A><B><a name="sec31subsec1" id="sec31subsec1"></A><a name="sec31" id="sec31"></A>31 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="31" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Commission may conduct an inquiry under this section for the purpose of carrying out its functions under this Act if the Commission believes it is in the public interest to do <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="4" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec4_smooth">so.  2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec31subsec2" id="sec31subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Conduct of inquiry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> An inquiry may be conducted under this section by any person who is appointed by the Commission to carry out inquiries under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec3" id="sec31subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Production of certificate</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry under this section shall produce proof of their appointment upon request.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec4" id="sec31subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Entry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry under this section may, without warrant, enter any lands or any building, structure or premises where the person has reason to believe there may be documents, things or information relevant to the inquiry.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec5" id="sec31subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Time of entry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> The power to enter a place under subsection (4) may be exercised only during the place’s regular business hours or, if it does not have regular business hours, during daylight hours.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec6" id="sec31subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Dwellings</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry under this section shall not enter into a place or part of a place that is a dwelling without the consent of the occupant.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec7" id="sec31subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Powers on inquiry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry may,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  request the production for inspection and examination of documents or things that are or may be relevant to the inquiry;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  upon giving a receipt for it, remove from a place documents produced in response to a request under clause (a) for the purpose of making copies or extracts; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  question a person on matters that are or may be relevant to the inquiry, subject to the person’s right to have counsel or a personal representative present during such questioning and exclude from the questioning any person who may be adverse in interest to the inquiry;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  use any data storage, processing or retrieval device or system used in carrying on business in the place in order to produce a document in readable form;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  take measurements or record by any means the physical dimensions of a place;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (f)  take photographs, video recordings or other visual or audio recordings of the interior or exterior of a place; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (g)  require that a place or part thereof not be disturbed for a reasonable period of time for the purposes of carrying out an examination, inquiry or test.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec8" id="sec31subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Written demand</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> A demand that a document or thing be produced must be in writing and must include a statement of the nature of the document or thing required.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec9" id="sec31subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Assistance</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry may be accompanied by any person who has special, expert or professional knowledge and who may be of assistance in carrying out the inquiry.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec10" id="sec31subsec10"></A><P class="headnote">Use of force prohibited</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="10" alinea="null">(10)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry shall not use force to enter and search premises under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec11" id="sec31subsec11"></A><P class="headnote">Obligation to produce and assist</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="11" alinea="null">(11)</SPAN> A person who is requested to produce a document or thing under clause (7) (a) shall produce it and shall, on request by the person conducting the inquiry, provide any assistance that is reasonably necessary, including assistance in using any data storage, processing or retrieval device or system, to produce a document in readable form.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec12" id="sec31subsec12"></A><P class="headnote">Return of removed things</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="12" alinea="null">(12)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry who removes any document or thing from a place under clause (7) (b) shall,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  make it available to the person from whom it was removed, on request, at a time and place convenient for both that person and the person conducting the inquiry; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  return it to the person from whom it was removed within a reasonable time.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec13" id="sec31subsec13"></A><P class="headnote">Admissibility of copies</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="13" alinea="null">(13)</SPAN> A copy of a document certified by a person conducting an inquiry to be a true copy of the original is admissible in evidence to the same extent as the original and has the same evidentiary value.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31subsec14" id="sec31subsec14"></A><P class="headnote">Obstruction</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31" subsection="14" alinea="null">(14)</SPAN> No person shall obstruct or interfere with a person conducting an inquiry under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Search warrant</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.1" data-viibes-start="34" data-viibes-end="33"><A name="BK36"></A><B><a name="sec31.1subsec1" id="sec31_1subsec1"></A><a name="sec31.1" id="sec31_1"></A>31.1</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Commission may authorize a person to apply to a justice of the peace for a warrant to enter a place and conduct a search of the place if,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  a person conducting an inquiry under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" href="#sec31_smooth">section 31</A> has been denied entry to any place or asked to leave a place before concluding a search;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  a person conducting an inquiry under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" href="#sec31_smooth">section 31</A> made a request for documents or things and the request was refused; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  an inquiry under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" href="#sec31_smooth">section 31</A> is otherwise obstructed or prevented.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec2" id="sec31_1subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Upon application by a person authorized under subsection (1) to do so, a justice of the peace may issue a warrant under this section if he or she is satisfied on information under oath or affirmation that the warrant is necessary for the purposes of carrying out the inquiry under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" href="#sec31_smooth">section 31</A>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec3" id="sec31_1subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Powers</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> A warrant obtained under subsection (2) may authorize a person named in the warrant, upon producing proof of his or her appointment, </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  to enter any place specified in the warrant, including a dwelling; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  to do any of the things specified in the warrant.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec4" id="sec31_1subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Conditions on search warrant</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> A warrant obtained under subsection (2) shall contain such conditions as the justice of the peace considers advisable to ensure that any search authorized by the warrant is reasonable in the circumstances.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec5" id="sec31_1subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Time of execution</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> An entry under a warrant issued under this section shall be made at such reasonable times as may be specified in the warrant.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec6" id="sec31_1subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Expiry of warrant</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> A warrant issued under this section shall name a date of expiry, which shall be no later than 15 days after the warrant is issued, but a justice of the peace may extend the date of expiry for an additional period of no more than 15 days, upon application without notice by the person named in the warrant.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec7" id="sec31_1subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Use of force</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> The person authorized to execute the warrant may call upon police officers for assistance in executing the warrant and the person may use whatever force is reasonably necessary to execute the warrant.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec8" id="sec31_1subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Obstruction prohibited</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> No person shall obstruct or hinder a person in the execution of a warrant issued under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.1subsec9" id="sec31_1subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Application</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.1" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" ss="11" href="#sec31subsec11_smooth">Subsections 31 (11)</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" ss="12" href="#sec31subsec12_smooth">(12)</A> and <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" ss="13" href="#sec31subsec13_smooth">(13)</A> apply with necessary modifications to an inquiry carried out pursuant to a warrant issued under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Evidence used in Tribunal proceedings</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.2" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.2" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.2"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.2" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.2" data-viibes-start="35" data-viibes-end="34"><A name="BK37"></A><B><a name="sec31.2" id="sec31_2"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="31.2" subsection="null" alinea="null">31.2</SPAN></B> Despite any other Act, evidence obtained on an inquiry under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" href="#sec31_smooth">section 31</A> or <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31.1" href="#sec31.1_smooth">31.1</A> may be received into evidence in a proceeding before the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Anti-Racism Secretariat</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.3" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.3" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.3"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.3" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.3" data-viibes-start="36" data-viibes-end="35"><A name="BK38"></A><B><a name="sec31.3subsec1" id="sec31_3subsec1"></A><a name="sec31.3" id="sec31_3"></A>31.3</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="31.3" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Chief Commissioner directs the Anti-Racism Secretariat which shall be established in accordance with subsection (2).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec31.3subsec2" id="sec31_3subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Composition</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.3" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Anti-Racism Secretariat shall be composed of not more than six persons appointed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council on the advice of the Chief Commissioner.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.3subsec3" id="sec31_3subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Remuneration</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.3" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council may fix the remuneration and allowance for expenses of the members of the Anti-Racism Secretariat.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.3subsec4" id="sec31_3subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Functions of the Secretariat</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.3" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> At the direction of the Chief Commissioner, the Anti-Racism Secretariat shall,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  undertake, direct and encourage research into discriminatory practices that infringe rights under Part I on the basis of racism or a related ground and make recommendations to the Commission designed to prevent and eliminate such discriminatory practices; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  facilitate the development and provision of programs of public information and education relating to the elimination of racism; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  undertake such tasks and responsibilities as may be assigned by the Chief Commissioner.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Disability Rights Secretariat</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.4" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.4" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.4"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.4" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.4" data-viibes-start="37" data-viibes-end="36"><A name="BK39"></A><B><a name="sec31.4subsec1" id="sec31_4subsec1"></A><a name="sec31.4" id="sec31_4"></A>31.4</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="31.4" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Chief Commissioner directs the Disability Rights Secretariat which shall be established in accordance with subsection (2).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec31.4subsec2" id="sec31_4subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Composition</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.4" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Disability Rights Secretariat shall be composed of not more than six persons appointed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council on the advice of the Chief Commissioner.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.4subsec3" id="sec31_4subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Remuneration</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.4" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council may fix the remuneration and allowance for expenses of the members of the Disability Rights Secretariat.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.4subsec4" id="sec31_4subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Functions of the Secretariat</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.4" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> At the direction of the Chief Commissioner, the Disability Rights Secretariat shall,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  undertake, direct and encourage research into discriminatory practices that infringe rights under Part I on the basis of disability and make recommendations to the Commission designed to prevent and eliminate such discriminatory practices; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  facilitate the development and provision of programs of public information and education intended to promote the elimination of discriminatory practices that infringe rights under Part I on the basis of disability; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  undertake such tasks and responsibilities as may be assigned by the Chief Commissioner.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Advisory groups</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.5" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.5" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.5"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.5" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.5" data-viibes-start="38" data-viibes-end="37"><A name="BK40"></A><B><a name="sec31.5" id="sec31_5"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="31.5" subsection="null" alinea="null">31.5</SPAN></B> The Chief Commissioner may establish such advisory groups as he or she considers appropriate to advise the Commission about the elimination of discriminatory practices that infringe rights under this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Annual report</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.6" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.6" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.6"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.6" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.6" data-viibes-start="39" data-viibes-end="38"><A name="BK41"></A><B><a name="sec31.6subsec1" id="sec31_6subsec1"></A><a name="sec31.6" id="sec31_6"></A>31.6</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="31.6" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Every year, the Commission shall prepare an annual report on the affairs of the Commission that occurred during the 12-month period ending on March 31 of each year.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec31.6subsec2" id="sec31_6subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Report to Speaker</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.6" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Commission shall submit the report to the Speaker of the Assembly no later than on June 30 in each year who shall cause the report to be laid before the Assembly if it is in session or, if not, at the next session.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec31.6subsec3" id="sec31_6subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Copy to Minister</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="31.6" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Commission shall give a copy of the report to the Minister at least 30 days before it is submitted to the Speaker under subsection (2).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Other reports</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="31.7" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec31.7" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=31.7"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="31.7" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="31.7" data-viibes-start="40" data-viibes-end="39"><A name="BK42"></A><B><a name="sec31.7" id="sec31_7"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="31.7" subsection="null" alinea="null">31.7</SPAN></B> In addition to the annual report, the Commission may make any other reports respecting the state of human rights in Ontario and the affairs of the Commission as it considers appropriate, and may present such reports to the public or any other person it considers appropriate.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 4</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<A name="part_iv_human_rights_tribunal_of_ontario_59686"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK43"></A>part iv <BR>  human rights tribunal of ontario</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Tribunal</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="32" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec32" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=32"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="32" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="21" data-noteup-count-display="21"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="32" data-viibes-start="41" data-viibes-end="40"><A name="BK44"></A><B><a name="sec32subsec1" id="sec32subsec1"></A><a name="sec32" id="sec32"></A>32 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="32" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Tribunal known as the Human Rights Tribunal of Ontario in English and Tribunal des droits de la personne de l’Ontario in French is continued.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec32subsec2" id="sec32subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Composition</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Tribunal shall be composed of such members as are appointed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council in accordance with the selection process described in subsection (3).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec3" id="sec32subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Selection process</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The selection process for the appointment of members of the Tribunal shall be a competitive process and the criteria to be applied in assessing candidates shall include the following:</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  Experience, knowledge or training with respect to human rights law and issues.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  Aptitude for impartial adjudication.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  3.  Aptitude for applying the alternative adjudicative practices and procedures that may be set out in the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec4" id="sec32subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Remuneration</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The members of the Tribunal shall be paid such remuneration and allowance for expenses as are fixed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec5" id="sec32subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Term of office</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> A member of the Tribunal shall be appointed for such term as may be specified by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec6" id="sec32subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Chair, vice-chair</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council shall appoint a chair and may appoint one or more vice-chairs of the Tribunal from among the members of the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec7" id="sec32subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Alternate chair</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council shall designate one of the vice-chairs to be the alternate chair.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec8" id="sec32subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> If the chair is unable to act, the alternate chair shall perform the duties of the chair and, for this purpose, has all the powers of the chair.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec9" id="sec32subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Employees</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> The Tribunal may appoint such employees as it considers necessary for the proper conduct of its affairs and the employees shall be appointed under Part III of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="825-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2006-c-35-sch-a/latest/so-2006-c-35-sch-a.html">Public Service of Ontario Act, 2006</A></I>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96728-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-35/latest/so-2006-c-35.html">2006, c. 35</A>, Sched. C, <SPAN class="reflex2-link" link-count="1" link1="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-35/latest/so-2006-c-35.html#sec132subsec6" title1="Public Service of Ontario Statute Law Amendment Act, 2006, SO 2006, c 35 (Ontario)" concatenated-id="96728" s="132" ss="6" data-link-type="weak">s. 132 (6)</SPAN>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec10" id="sec32subsec10"></A><P class="headnote">Evidence obtained in course of proceeding</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="10" alinea="null">(10)</SPAN> A member or employee of the Tribunal shall not be required to give testimony in a civil suit or any proceeding as to information obtained in the course of a proceeding before the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec32subsec11" id="sec32subsec11"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="32" subsection="11" alinea="null">(11)</SPAN> Despite subsection (10), an employee of the Tribunal may be required to give testimony in a proceeding before the Tribunal in the circumstances prescribed by the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Panels</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="33" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec33" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=33"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="33" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="26" data-noteup-count-display="26"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="33" data-viibes-start="42" data-viibes-end="41"><A name="BK45"></A><B><a name="sec33subsec1" id="sec33subsec1"></A><a name="sec33" id="sec33"></A>33 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="33" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The chair of the Tribunal may appoint panels composed of one or more members of the Tribunal to exercise and perform the powers and duties of the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec33subsec2" id="sec33subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Person designated to preside over panel</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="33" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> If a panel of the Tribunal holds a hearing, the chair of the Tribunal shall designate one member of the panel to preside over the hearing.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec33subsec3" id="sec33subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Reassignment of panel</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="33" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> If a panel of the Tribunal is unable for any reason to exercise or perform the powers or duties of the Tribunal, the chair of the Tribunal may assign another panel in its place.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Application by person</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="34" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec34" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=34"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="34" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="6602" data-noteup-count-display="6.6k"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="34" data-viibes-start="43" data-viibes-end="42"><A name="BK46"></A><B><a name="sec34subsec1" id="sec34subsec1"></A><a name="sec34" id="sec34"></A>34 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="34" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> If a person believes that any of his or her rights under Part I<B> </B>have been infringed, the person may apply to the Tribunal for an order under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.2" href="#sec45.2_smooth">section 45.2</A>,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  within one year after the incident to which the application relates; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  if there was a series of incidents, within one year after the last incident in the series.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec2" id="sec34subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Late applications </P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> A person may apply under subsection (1) after the expiry of the time limit under that subsection if the Tribunal is satisfied that the delay was incurred in good faith and no substantial prejudice will result to any person affected by the delay.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec3" id="sec34subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Form</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> An application under subsection (1) shall be in a form approved by the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec4" id="sec34subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Two or more persons</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> Two or more persons who are each entitled to make an application under subsection (1) may file the applications jointly, subject to any provision in the Tribunal rules that authorizes the Tribunal to direct that one or more of the applications be considered in a separate proceeding.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec5" id="sec34subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Application on behalf of another</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> A person or organization, other than the Commission, may apply on behalf of another person to the Tribunal for an order under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.2" href="#sec45.2_smooth">section 45.2</A> if the other person,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  would have been entitled to bring an application under subsection (1); and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  consents to the application.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec6" id="sec34subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Participation in proceedings</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> If a person or organization makes an application on behalf of another person, the person or organization may participate in the proceeding in accordance with the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec7" id="sec34subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Consent form</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> A consent under clause (5) (b) shall be in a form specified in the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec8" id="sec34subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Time of application</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> An application under subsection (5) shall be made within the time period required for making an application under subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec9" id="sec34subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Application </P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> Subsections (2) and (3) apply to an application made under subsection (5).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec10" id="sec34subsec10"></A><P class="headnote">Withdrawal of application</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="10" alinea="null">(10)</SPAN> An application under subsection (5) may be withdrawn by the person on behalf of whom the application is made in accordance with the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec11" id="sec34subsec11"></A><P class="headnote">Where application barred</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="11" alinea="null">(11)</SPAN> A person who believes that one of his or her rights under Part I has been infringed may not make an application under subsection (1) with respect to that right if,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  a civil proceeding has been commenced in a court in which the person is seeking an order under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="46.1" href="#sec46.1_smooth">section 46.1</A> with respect to the alleged infringement and the proceeding has not been finally determined or withdrawn; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  a court has finally determined the issue of whether the right has been infringed or the matter has been settled.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec34subsec12" id="sec34subsec12"></A><P class="headnote">Final determination</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="34" subsection="12" alinea="null">(12)</SPAN> For the purpose of subsection (11), a proceeding or issue has not been finally determined if a right of appeal exists and the time for appealing has not expired.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Application by Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="35" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec35" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=35"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="35" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="50" data-noteup-count-display="50"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="35" data-viibes-start="44" data-viibes-end="43"><A name="BK47"></A><B><a name="sec35subsec1" id="sec35subsec1"></A><a name="sec35" id="sec35"></A>35 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="35" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Commission may apply to the Tribunal for an order under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.3" href="#sec45.3_smooth">section 45.3</A> if the Commission is of the opinion that,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  it is in the public interest to make an application; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  an order under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.3" href="#sec45.3_smooth">section 45.3</A> could provide an appropriate remedy.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec35subsec2" id="sec35subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Form</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="35" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> An application under subsection (1) shall be in a form approved by the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec35subsec3" id="sec35subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Effect of application</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="35" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> An application made by the Commission does not affect the right of a person to make an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> in respect of the same matter.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec35subsec4" id="sec35subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Applications dealt with together</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="35" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> If a person or organization makes an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> and the Commission makes an application under this section in respect of the same matter, the two applications shall be dealt with together in the same proceeding unless the Tribunal determines otherwise.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Parties</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="36" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec36" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=36"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="36" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="75" data-noteup-count-display="75"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="36" data-viibes-start="45" data-viibes-end="44"><A name="BK48"></A><B><a name="sec36" id="sec36"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="36" subsection="null" alinea="null">36</SPAN> </B>The parties to an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> or<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth"> 35</A> are the following:</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  In the case of an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" ss="1" href="#sec34subsec1_smooth">subsection 34 (1)</A>, the person who made the application.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  In the case of an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" ss="5" href="#sec34subsec5_smooth">subsection 34 (5)</A>, the person on behalf of whom the application is made.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  3.  In the case of an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth">section 35</A>, the Commission.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  4.  Any person against whom an order is sought in the application.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  5.  Any other person or the Commission, if they are added as a party by the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Intervention by Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="37" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec37" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=37"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="37" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="50" data-noteup-count-display="50"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="37" data-viibes-start="46" data-viibes-end="45"><A name="BK49"></A><B><a name="sec37subsec1" id="sec37subsec1"></A><a name="sec37" id="sec37"></A>37 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="37" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Commission may intervene in an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> on such terms as the Tribunal may determine having regard to the role and mandate of the Commission under this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec37subsec2" id="sec37subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Intervention as a party</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="37" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Commission may intervene as a party to an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> if the person or organization who made the application consents to the intervention as a party.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Disclosure of information to Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="38" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec38" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=38"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="38" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="18" data-noteup-count-display="18"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="38" data-viibes-start="47" data-viibes-end="46"><A name="BK50"></A><B><a name="sec38" id="sec38"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="38" subsection="null" alinea="null">38</SPAN> </B>Despite anything in the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="169-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-f31/latest/rso-1990-c-f31.html">Freedom of Information and Protection of Privacy Act</A></I>, at the request of the Commission, the Tribunal shall disclose to the Commission copies of applications and responses filed with the Tribunal and may disclose to the Commission other documents in its custody or in its control.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Powers of Tribunal</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="39" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec39" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=39"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="39" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="68" data-noteup-count-display="68"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="39" data-viibes-start="48" data-viibes-end="47"><A name="BK51"></A><B><a name="sec39" id="sec39"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="39" subsection="null" alinea="null">39</SPAN> </B>The Tribunal has the jurisdiction to exercise the powers conferred on it by or under this Act and to determine all questions of fact or law that arise in any application before it.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Disposition of applications</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="40" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec40" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=40"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="40" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="90" data-noteup-count-display="90"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="40" data-viibes-start="49" data-viibes-end="48"><A name="BK52"></A><B><a name="sec40" id="sec40"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="40" subsection="null" alinea="null">40</SPAN> </B>The Tribunal shall dispose of applications made under this Part by adopting the procedures and practices provided for in its rules or otherwise available to the Tribunal which, in its opinion, offer the best opportunity for a fair, just and expeditious resolution of the merits of the applications.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Interpretation of Part and rules</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="41" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec41" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=41"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="41" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="174" data-noteup-count-display="174"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="41" data-viibes-start="50" data-viibes-end="49"><A name="BK53"></A><B><a name="sec41" id="sec41"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="41" subsection="null" alinea="null">41</SPAN> </B>This Part and the Tribunal rules shall be liberally construed to permit the Tribunal to adopt practices and procedures, including alternatives to traditional adjudicative or adversarial procedures that, in the opinion of the Tribunal, will facilitate fair, just and expeditious resolutions of the merits of the matters before it.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="41.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec41.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=41.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="41.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="41.1" data-viibes-start="51" data-viibes-end="50"><B><a name="sec41.1" id="sec41_1"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="41.1" subsection="null" alinea="null">41.1</SPAN></B> Repealed: 1995, c. 4, s. 3 (3).</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote"><I>Statutory Powers Procedure Act</I></P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="42" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec42" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=42"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="42" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="55" data-noteup-count-display="55"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="42" data-viibes-start="52" data-viibes-end="51"><A name="BK54"></A><B><a name="sec42subsec1" id="sec42subsec1"></A><a name="sec42" id="sec42"></A>42 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="42" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The provisions of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="474-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-s22/latest/rso-1990-c-s22.html">Statutory Powers Procedure Act</A></I> apply to a proceeding before the Tribunal unless they conflict with a provision of this Act, the regulations or the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec42subsec2" id="sec42subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Conflict</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="42" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Despite <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" href="#sec32_smooth">section 32</A> of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="474-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-s22/latest/rso-1990-c-s22.html">Statutory Powers Procedure Act</A></I>, this Act, the regulations and the Tribunal rules prevail over the provisions of that Act with which they conflict.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Tribunal rules</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="43" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec43" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=43"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="43" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="150" data-noteup-count-display="150"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="43" data-viibes-start="53" data-viibes-end="52"><A name="BK55"></A><B><a name="sec43subsec1" id="sec43subsec1"></A><a name="sec43" id="sec43"></A>43 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="43" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Tribunal may make rules governing the practice and procedure before it.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec43subsec2" id="sec43subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Required practices and procedures</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The rules shall ensure that the following requirements are met with respect to any proceeding before the Tribunal:</P>
