<P class="paragraph">  1.  An application that is within the jurisdiction of the Tribunal shall not be finally disposed of without affording the parties an opportunity to make oral submissions in accordance with the rules.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  An application may not be finally disposed of without written reasons.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec3" id="sec43subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Without limiting the generality of subsection (1), the Tribunal rules may,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  provide for and require the use of hearings or of practices and procedures that are provided for under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="474-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-s22/latest/rso-1990-c-s22.html">Statutory Powers Procedure Act</A></I> or that are alternatives to traditional adjudicative or adversarial procedures; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  authorize the Tribunal to,</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (i)  define or narrow the issues required to dispose of an application and limit the evidence and submissions of the parties on such issues, and</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (ii)  determine the order in which the issues and evidence in a proceeding will be presented;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  authorize the Tribunal to conduct examinations in chief or cross-examinations of a witness;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  prescribe the stages of its processes at which preliminary, procedural or interlocutory matters will be determined;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  authorize the Tribunal to make or cause to be made such examinations of records and such other inquiries as it considers necessary in the circumstances;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (f)  authorize the Tribunal to require a party to a proceeding or another person to,</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (i)  produce any document, information or thing and provide such assistance as is reasonably necessary, including using any data storage, processing or retrieval device or system, to produce the information in any form,</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (ii)  provide a statement or oral or affidavit evidence, or</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (iii)  in the case of a party to the proceeding, adduce evidence or produce witnesses who are reasonably within the party’s control; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (g)  govern any matter prescribed by the regulations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec4" id="sec43subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">General or particular</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The rules may be of general or particular application.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec5" id="sec43subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Consistency</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> The rules shall be consistent with this Part.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec6" id="sec43subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Not a regulation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> The rules made under this section are not regulations for the purposes of Part III of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="814-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2006-c-21-sch-f/latest/so-2006-c-21-sch-f.html">Legislation Act, 2006</A></I>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, ss. 5, 11</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec7" id="sec43subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Public consultations</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> The Tribunal shall hold public consultations before making a rule under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec8" id="sec43subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Failure to comply with rules</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> Failure on the part of the Tribunal to comply with the practices and procedures required by the rules or the exercise of a discretion under the rules by the Tribunal in a particular manner is not a ground for setting aside a decision of the Tribunal on an application for judicial review or any other form of relief, unless the failure or the exercise of a discretion caused a substantial wrong which affected the final disposition of the matter.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec43subsec9" id="sec43subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Adverse inference</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="43" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> The Tribunal may draw an adverse inference from the failure of a party to comply, in whole or in part, with an order of the Tribunal for the party to do anything under a rule made under clause (3) (f).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Tribunal inquiry</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="44" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec44" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=44"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="44" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="32" data-noteup-count-display="32"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="44" data-viibes-start="54" data-viibes-end="53"><A name="BK56"></A><B><a name="sec44subsec1" id="sec44subsec1"></A><a name="sec44" id="sec44"></A>44 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="44" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> At the request of a party to an application under this Part, the Tribunal may appoint a person to conduct an inquiry under this section if the Tribunal is satisfied that,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  an inquiry is required in order to obtain evidence;
</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  the evidence obtained may assist in achieving a fair, just and expeditious resolution of the merits of the application; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  it is appropriate to do so in the circumstances.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec2" id="sec44subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Production of certificate</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry under this section shall produce proof of their appointment upon request.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec3" id="sec44subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Entry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry under this section may, without warrant, enter any lands or any building, structure or premises where the person has reason to believe there may be evidence relevant to the application.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec4" id="sec44subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Time of entry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The power to enter a place under subsection (3) may be exercised only during the place’s regular business hours or, if it does not have regular business hours, during daylight hours.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec5" id="sec44subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Dwellings</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry shall not enter into a place or part of a place that is a dwelling without the consent of the occupant.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec6" id="sec44subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Powers on inquiry</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry may,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  request the production for inspection and examination of documents or things that are or may be relevant to the inquiry;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  upon giving a receipt for it, remove from a place documents produced in response to a request under clause (a) for the purpose of making copies or extracts; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  question a person on matters that are or may be relevant to the inquiry, subject to the person’s right to have counsel or a personal representative present during such questioning and exclude from the questioning any person who may be adverse in interest to the inquiry;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  use any data storage, processing or retrieval device or system used in carrying on business in the place in order to produce a document in readable form;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  take measurements or record by any means the physical dimensions of a place;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (f)  take photographs, video recordings or other visual or audio recordings of the interior or exterior of a place; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (g)  require that a place or part thereof not be disturbed for a reasonable period of time for the purposes of carrying out an examination, inquiry or test.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec7" id="sec44subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Written demand</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> A demand that a document or thing be produced must be in writing and must include a statement of the nature of the document or thing required.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec8" id="sec44subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Assistance</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry may be accompanied by any person who has special, expert or professional knowledge and who may be of assistance in carrying out the inquiry.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec9" id="sec44subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Use of force prohibited</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry shall not use force to enter and search premises under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec10" id="sec44subsec10"></A><P class="headnote">Obligation to produce and assist</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="10" alinea="null">(10)</SPAN> A person who is requested to produce a document or thing under clause (6) (a) shall produce it and shall, on request by the person conducting the inquiry, provide any assistance that is reasonably necessary, including assistance in using any data storage, processing or retrieval device or system, to produce a document in readable form.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec11" id="sec44subsec11"></A><P class="headnote">Return of removed things</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="11" alinea="null">(11)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry who removes any document or thing from a place under clause (6) (b) shall,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  make it available to the person from whom it was removed, on request, at a time and place convenient for both that person and the person conducting the inquiry; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  return it to the person from whom it was removed within a reasonable time.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec12" id="sec44subsec12"></A><P class="headnote">Admissibility of copies</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="12" alinea="null">(12)</SPAN> A copy of a document certified by a person conducting an inquiry to be a true copy of the original is admissible in evidence to the same extent as the original and has the same evidentiary value.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec13" id="sec44subsec13"></A><P class="headnote">Obstruction</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="13" alinea="null">(13)</SPAN> No person shall obstruct or interfere with a person conducting an inquiry under this section.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec14" id="sec44subsec14"></A><P class="headnote">Inquiry report</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="14" alinea="null">(14)</SPAN> A person conducting an inquiry shall prepare a report and submit it to the Tribunal and the parties to the application that gave rise to the inquiry in accordance with the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec44subsec15" id="sec44subsec15"></A><P class="headnote">Transfer of inquiry to Commission</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="44" subsection="15" alinea="null">(15)</SPAN> The Commission may, at the request of the Tribunal, appoint a person to conduct an inquiry under this section and the person so appointed has all of the powers of a person appointed by the Tribunal under this section and shall report to the Tribunal in accordance with subsection (14).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Deferral of application</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="538" data-noteup-count-display="538"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45" data-viibes-start="55" data-viibes-end="54"><A name="BK57"></A><B><a name="sec45" id="sec45"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45" subsection="null" alinea="null">45</SPAN> </B>The Tribunal may defer an application in accordance with the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Dismissal in accordance with rules</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1311" data-noteup-count-display="1.3k"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.1" data-viibes-start="56" data-viibes-end="55"><A name="BK58"></A><B><a name="sec45.1" id="sec45_1"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45.1" subsection="null" alinea="null">45.1</SPAN></B> The Tribunal may dismiss an application, in whole or in part, in accordance with its rules if the Tribunal is of the opinion that another proceeding has appropriately dealt with the substance of the application.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Orders of Tribunal:  applications under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">s. 34</A></P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.2" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.2" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.2"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.2" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="369" data-noteup-count-display="369"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.2" data-viibes-start="57" data-viibes-end="56"><A name="BK59"></A><B><a name="sec45.2subsec1" id="sec45_2subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.2" id="sec45_2"></A>45.2</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.2" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> On an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A>, the Tribunal may make one or more of the following orders if the Tribunal determines that a party to the application<B> </B>has infringed a right under Part I of another party to the application:</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  An order directing the party who infringed the right to pay monetary compensation to the party whose right was infringed for loss arising out of the infringement, including compensation for injury to dignity, feelings and self-respect.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  An order directing the party who infringed the right to make restitution to the party whose right was infringed, other than through monetary compensation, for loss arising out of the infringement, including restitution for injury to dignity, feelings and self-respect.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  3.  An order directing any party to the application to do anything that, in the opinion of the Tribunal, the party ought to do to promote compliance with this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.2subsec2" id="sec45_2subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Orders under par. 3 of subs. (1)</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.2" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> For greater certainty, an order under paragraph 3 of subsection (1),</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  may direct a person to do anything with respect to future practices; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  may be made even if no order under that paragraph was requested.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Orders of Tribunal: applications under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth">s. 35</A></P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.3" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.3" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.3"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.3" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="3" data-noteup-count-display="3"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.3" data-viibes-start="58" data-viibes-end="57"><A name="BK60"></A><B><a name="sec45.3subsec1" id="sec45_3subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.3" id="sec45_3"></A>45.3</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.3" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> If, on an application under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth">section 35</A>, the Tribunal determines that any one or more of the parties to the application have infringed a right under Part I, the Tribunal may make an order directing any party to the application to do anything that, in the opinion of the Tribunal, the party ought to do to promote compliance with this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.3subsec2" id="sec45_3subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.3" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> For greater certainty, an order under subsection (1) may direct a person to do anything with respect to future practices.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Matters referred to Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.4" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.4" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.4"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.4" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="2" data-noteup-count-display="2"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.4" data-viibes-start="59" data-viibes-end="58"><A name="BK61"></A><B><a name="sec45.4subsec1" id="sec45_4subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.4" id="sec45_4"></A>45.4</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.4" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Tribunal may refer any matters arising out of a proceeding before it to the Commission if, in the Tribunal’s opinion, they are matters of public interest or are otherwise of interest to the Commission.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.4subsec2" id="sec45_4subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.4" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Commission may, in its discretion, decide whether to deal with a matter referred to it by the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Documents published by Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.5" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.5" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.5"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.5" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="29" data-noteup-count-display="29"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.5" data-viibes-start="60" data-viibes-end="59"><A name="BK62"></A><B><a name="sec45.5subsec1" id="sec45_5subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.5" id="sec45_5"></A>45.5</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.5" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> In a proceeding under this Part, the Tribunal may consider policies approved by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="30" href="#sec30_smooth">section 30</A>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.5subsec2" id="sec45_5subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.5" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Despite subsection (1), the Tribunal shall consider a policy approved by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="30" href="#sec30_smooth">section 30</A> in a proceeding under this Part if a party to the proceeding or an intervenor requests that it do <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="5" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec5_smooth">so.  2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Stated case to Divisional court</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.6" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.6" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.6"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.6" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="2" data-noteup-count-display="2"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.6" data-viibes-start="61" data-viibes-end="60"><A name="BK63"></A><B><a name="sec45.6subsec1" id="sec45_6subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.6" id="sec45_6"></A>45.6</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> If the Tribunal makes a final decision or order in a proceeding in which the Commission was a party or an intervenor, and the Commission believes that the decision or order is not consistent with a policy that has been approved by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="30" href="#sec30_smooth">section 30</A>, the Commission may apply to the Tribunal to have the Tribunal state a case to the Divisional Court.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.6subsec2" id="sec45_6subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> If the Tribunal determines that the application of the Commission relates to a question of law and that it is appropriate to do so, it may state the case in writing for the opinion of the Divisional Court upon the question of law.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.6subsec3" id="sec45_6subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Parties</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The parties to a stated case under this section are the parties to the proceeding referred to in subsection (1) and, if the Commission was an intervenor in that proceeding, the Commission.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.6subsec4" id="sec45_6subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Submissions by Tribunal</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The Divisional Court may hear submissions from the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.6subsec5" id="sec45_6subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Powers of Divisional Court</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> The Divisional Court shall hear and determine the stated case.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.6subsec6" id="sec45_6subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">No stay</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> Unless otherwise ordered by the Tribunal or the Divisional Court, an application by the Commission under subsection (1) or the stating of a case to the Divisional Court under subsection (2) does not operate as a stay of the final decision or order of the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.6subsec7" id="sec45_6subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Reconsideration of Tribunal decision</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.6" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> Within 30 days of receipt of the decision of the Divisional Court, any party to the stated case proceeding may apply to the Tribunal for a reconsideration of its original decision or order in accordance with <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.7" href="#sec45.7_smooth">section 45.7</A>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Reconsideration of Tribunal decision</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.7" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.7" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.7"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.7" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="546" data-noteup-count-display="546"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.7" data-viibes-start="62" data-viibes-end="61"><A name="BK64"></A><B><a name="sec45.7subsec1" id="sec45_7subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.7" id="sec45_7"></A>45.7</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.7" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Any party to a proceeding before the Tribunal may request that the Tribunal reconsider its decision in accordance with the Tribunal rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.7subsec2" id="sec45_7subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.7" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Upon request under subsection (1) or on its own motion, the Tribunal may reconsider its decision in accordance with its rules.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Decisions final</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.8" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.8" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.8"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.8" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="59" data-noteup-count-display="59"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.8" data-viibes-start="63" data-viibes-end="62"><A name="BK65"></A><B><a name="sec45.8" id="sec45_8"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45.8" subsection="null" alinea="null">45.8</SPAN></B> Subject to <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.7" href="#sec45.7_smooth">section 45.7</A> of this Act, section 21.1 of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="474-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-s22/latest/rso-1990-c-s22.html">Statutory Powers Procedure Act</A></I> and the Tribunal rules, a decision of the Tribunal is final and not subject to appeal and shall not be altered or set aside in an application for judicial review or in any other proceeding unless the decision is patently unreasonable.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96804-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2009-c-33/latest/so-2009-c-33.html">2009, c. 33</A>, Sched. 2, s. 35 (3).</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Settlements</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.9" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.9" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.9"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.9" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="330" data-noteup-count-display="330"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.9" data-viibes-start="64" data-viibes-end="63"><A name="BK66"></A><B><a name="sec45.9subsec1" id="sec45_9subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.9" id="sec45_9"></A>45.9</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> If a settlement of an application made under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> or<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth"> 35</A> is agreed to in writing and signed by the parties, the settlement is binding on the parties.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec2" id="sec45_9subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Consent order</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> If a settlement of an application made under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> or<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth"> 35</A> is agreed to in writing and signed by the parties, the Tribunal may, on the joint motion of the parties, make an order requiring compliance with the settlement or any part of the settlement.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec3" id="sec45_9subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Application where contravention</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> If a settlement of an application made under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">section 34</A> or<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="35" href="#sec35_smooth"> 35</A> is agreed to in writing and signed by the parties, a party who believes that another party has contravened the settlement may make an application to the Tribunal for an order under subsection (8),</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  within six months after the contravention to which the application relates; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  if there was a series of contraventions, within six months after the last contravention in the series.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec4" id="sec45_9subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Late applications </P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> A person may apply under subsection (3) after the expiry of the time limit under that subsection if the Tribunal is satisfied that the delay was incurred in good faith and no substantial prejudice will result to any person affected by the delay.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec5" id="sec45_9subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Form of application</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> An application under subsection (3) shall be in a form approved by the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec6" id="sec45_9subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Parties</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> Subject to the Tribunal rules, the parties to an application under subsection (3) are the following:</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  The parties to the settlement.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  Any other person or the Commission, if they are added as a party by the Tribunal.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec7" id="sec45_9subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Intervention by Commission</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="37" href="#sec37_smooth">Section 37</A> applies with necessary modifications to an application under subsection (3).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.9subsec8" id="sec45_9subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Order</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.9" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> If, on an application under subsection (3), the Tribunal determines that a party has contravened the settlement, the Tribunal may make any order that it considers appropriate to remedy the contravention.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 5</A>.</P>
 

 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.10" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.10" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.10"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.10" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1" data-noteup-count-display="1"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.10" data-viibes-start="65" data-viibes-end="64"><B><a name="sec45.10" id="sec45_10"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45.10" subsection="null" alinea="null">45.10</SPAN></B> Repealed: <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (1).</P></div>
 

 
<A name="part_iv_1_Human_rights_legal_support_centre_92315"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK67"></A>part iv.1 <BR>  Human rights legal support centre</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Centre established</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.11" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.11" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.11"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.11" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="2" data-noteup-count-display="2"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.11" data-viibes-start="66" data-viibes-end="65"><A name="BK68"></A><B><a name="sec45.11subsec1" id="sec45_11subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.11" id="sec45_11"></A>45.11 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.11" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> A corporation without share capital is established under the name Human Rights Legal Support Centre in English and Centre d’assistance juridique en matière de droits de la personne in French.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.11subsec2" id="sec45_11subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Membership</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.11" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The members of the Centre shall consist of its board of directors.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.11subsec3" id="sec45_11subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Not a Crown agency</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.11" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Centre is not an agent of Her Majesty nor a Crown agent for the purposes of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="94-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-c48/latest/rso-1990-c-c48.html">Crown Agency Act</A></I>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.11subsec4" id="sec45_11subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Powers of natural person</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.11" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The Centre has the capacity and the rights, powers and privileges of a natural person, subject to the limitations set out in this Act or the regulations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<P class="Pnote">Note: On a day to be named by proclamation of the Lieutenant Governor, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.11" ss="4" href="#sec45.11subsec4_smooth">subsection 45.11 (4)</A> of the Code is amended by adding “and to any limits imposed by section 11.0.1 of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="35251-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2011-c-9-sch-27/latest/so-2011-c-9-sch-27.html">Ministry of Infrastructure Act, 2011</A></I>” at the end. (See: 2023, c. 5, Sched. 2, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="10" href="#sec10_smooth">s. 10</A>)</P>
 
<a name="sec45.11subsec5" id="sec45_11subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Independent from but accountable to Ontario</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.11" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> The Centre shall be independent from, but accountable to, the Government of Ontario as set out in this Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Objects</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.12" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.12" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.12"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.12" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.12" data-viibes-start="67" data-viibes-end="66"><A name="BK69"></A><B><a name="sec45.12" id="sec45_12"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45.12" subsection="null" alinea="null">45.12</SPAN></B> The objects of the Centre are,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  to establish and administer a cost-effective and efficient system for providing support services, including legal services, respecting applications to the Tribunal under Part IV;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  to establish policies and priorities for the provision of support services based on its financial resources.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Provision of support services</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.13" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.13" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.13"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.13" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.13" data-viibes-start="68" data-viibes-end="67"><A name="BK70"></A><B><a name="sec45.13subsec1" id="sec45_13subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.13" id="sec45_13"></A>45.13</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.13" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Centre shall provide the following support services:</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  Advice and assistance, legal and otherwise, respecting the infringement of rights under Part I.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  Legal services in relation to, </P>
 
<P class="subpara">  i.  the making of applications to the Tribunal under Part IV,</P>
 
<P class="subpara">  ii.  proceedings before the Tribunal under Part IV,</P>
 
<P class="subpara">  iii.  applications for judicial review arising from Tribunal proceedings,</P>
 
<P class="subpara">  iv.  stated case proceedings,</P>
 
<P class="subpara">  v.  the enforcement of Tribunal orders.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  3.  Such other services as may be prescribed by regulation.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.13subsec2" id="sec45_13subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Availability of services</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.13" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Centre shall ensure that the support services are available throughout the Province, using such methods of delivering the services as the Centre believes are appropriate.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Board of directors</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.14" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.14" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.14"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.14" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1" data-noteup-count-display="1"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.14" data-viibes-start="69" data-viibes-end="68"><A name="BK71"></A><B><a name="sec45.14subsec1" id="sec45_14subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.14" id="sec45_14"></A>45.14</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The affairs of the Centre shall be governed and managed by its board of directors.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec2" id="sec45_14subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Composition and appointment</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The board of directors of the Centre shall consist of no fewer than five and no more than nine members appointed by the Lieutenant Governor in Council in accordance with the regulations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec3" id="sec45_14subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Appointment of Chair </P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> A Chair designated by the Lieutenant Governor in Council will preside at meetings.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec4" id="sec45_14subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Remuneration</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The board of directors may be remunerated as determined by the Lieutenant Governor in Council.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec5" id="sec45_14subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Duties</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> The board of directors of the Centre shall be responsible for furthering the objects of the Centre.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec6" id="sec45_14subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">Delegation</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> The board of directors may delegate any power or duty to any committee, to any member of a committee or to any officer or employee of the Centre.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec7" id="sec45_14subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> A delegation shall be in writing and shall be on the terms and subject to the limitations, conditions or requirements specified in it.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec8" id="sec45_14subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Board to act responsibly</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> The board of directors shall act in a financially responsible and accountable manner in exercising its powers and performing its duties.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.14subsec9" id="sec45_14subsec9"></A><P class="headnote">Standard of care</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.14" subsection="9" alinea="null">(9)</SPAN> Members of the board of directors shall act in good faith with a view to the objects of the Centre and shall exercise the care, diligence and skill of a reasonably prudent person.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Government funding</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.15" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.15" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.15"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.15" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.15" data-viibes-start="70" data-viibes-end="69"><A name="BK72"></A><B><a name="sec45.15subsec1" id="sec45_15subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.15" id="sec45_15"></A>45.15</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.15" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Centre shall submit its annual budget to the Minister for approval every year in a manner and form, and at a time, specified in the regulations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.15subsec2" id="sec45_15subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Approved budget included in estimates</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.15" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> If approved by the Minister, the annual budget shall be submitted to Cabinet to be reviewed for inclusion in the estimates of the Ministry.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec45.15subsec3" id="sec45_15subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Appropriation by Legislature</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.15" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The money required for the purposes of this Act shall be paid out of such money as is appropriated therefor by the Legislature.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Centre’s money not part of Consolidated Revenue Fund</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.16" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.16" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.16"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.16" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.16" data-viibes-start="71" data-viibes-end="70"><A name="BK73"></A><B><a name="sec45.16" id="sec45_16"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45.16" subsection="null" alinea="null">45.16</SPAN></B> The Centre’s money and investments do not form part of the Consolidated Revenue Fund and shall be used by the Centre in carrying out its objects.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Fiscal year</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.17" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.17" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.17"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.17" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.17" data-viibes-start="72" data-viibes-end="71"><A name="BK74"></A><B><a name="sec45.17" id="sec45_17"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="45.17" subsection="null" alinea="null">45.17</SPAN> </B>The fiscal year of the Centre shall be from April 1 to March 31 of the following year. <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (2).</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Annual report</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.17.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.17.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.17.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.17.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.17.1" data-viibes-start="73" data-viibes-end="72"><A name="BK75"></A><B><a name="sec45.17.1subsec1" id="sec45_17_1subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.17.1" id="sec45_17_1"></A>45.17.1 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.17.1" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Centre shall prepare an annual report, provide it to the Minister no later than 120 days after the end of the Centre’s fiscal year and make it available to the public. <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (2).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.17.1subsec2" id="sec45_17_1subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.17.1" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Centre shall comply with such directives as may be issued by the Management Board of Cabinet with respect to,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  the form and content of the annual report; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  when and how to make it available to the public. <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (2).</P>
 
<a name="sec45.17.1subsec3" id="sec45_17_1subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.17.1" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Centre shall include such additional content in the annual report as the Minister may require. <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (2).</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Audit </P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="45.18" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec45.18" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=45.18"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="45.18" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="45.18" data-viibes-start="74" data-viibes-end="73"><A name="BK76"></A><B><a name="sec45.18subsec1" id="sec45_18subsec1"></A><a name="sec45.18" id="sec45_18"></A>45.18</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="45.18" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Centre must ensure that its books of financial account are audited annually in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles and a copy of the audit is given to the Minister.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec45.18subsec2" id="sec45_18subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Audit by Minister</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="45.18" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> The Minister has the right to audit the Centre at any time that the Minister chooses.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 6</A>.</P>
 

 
<A name="PART_V_GENERAL_100219"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK77"></A>PART V <BR>  GENERAL</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Definitions, general</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="46" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec46" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=46"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="46" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="31" data-noteup-count-display="31"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="46" data-viibes-start="75" data-viibes-end="74"><A name="BK78"></A><B><a name="sec46" id="sec46"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="46" subsection="null" alinea="null">46</SPAN> </B>In this Act,</P></div>
 
<P class="definition">“Commission” means the Ontario Human Rights Commission; (“Commission”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“Minister” means the member of the Executive Council to whom the powers and duties of the Minister under this Act are assigned by the Lieutenant Governor in Council; (“ministre”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“person” in addition to the extended meaning given it by Part VI (Interpretation) of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="814-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2006-c-21-sch-f/latest/so-2006-c-21-sch-f.html">Legislation Act, 2006</A></I>, includes an employment agency, an employers’ organization, an unincorporated association, a trade or occupational association, a trade union, a partnership, a municipality, a board of police commissioners established under the <I>Police Act</I>, being chapter 381 of the Revised Statutes of Ontario, 1980, and a police services board established under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="377-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-p15/latest/rso-1990-c-p15.html">Police Services Act</A></I>; (“personne”)</P>
 
<P class="Pnote-e">Note: On a day to be named by proclamation of the Lieutenant Governor, the definition of “person” in section 46 of the Act is amended by striking out “police services board established under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="377-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-p15/latest/rso-1990-c-p15.html">Police Services Act</A></I>” and substituting “police service board established under the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="48744-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2019-c-1-sch-1/latest/so-2019-c-1-sch-1.html">Community Safety and Policing Act, 2019</A></I>”. (See: <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97025-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2019-c-1/latest/so-2019-c-1.html">2019, c. 1</A>, Sched. 4, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="25" href="#sec25_smooth">s. 25</A>)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“regulations” means the regulations made under this Act; (“règlements”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“Tribunal” means the Human Rights Tribunal of Ontario continued under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" href="#sec32_smooth">section 32</A>; (“Tribunal”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“Tribunal rules” means the rules governing practice and procedure that are made by the Tribunal under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="43" href="#sec43_smooth">section 43</A>. (“règles du Tribunal”)  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 46; 1994, c. 27, s. 65 (24); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96598-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2002-c-18/latest/so-2002-c-18.html">2002, c. 18</A>, Sched. C, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="7" href="#sec7_smooth">s. 7</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96714-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-21/latest/so-2006-c-21.html">2006, c. 21</A>, Sched. F, <SPAN class="reflex2-link" link-count="1" link1="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-21/latest/so-2006-c-21.html#sec136subsec2" title1="Access to Justice Act, 2006, SO 2006, c 21 (Ontario)" concatenated-id="96714" s="136" ss="2" data-link-type="weak">s. 136 (2)</SPAN>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 7</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Civil remedy</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="46.1" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec46.1" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=46.1"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="46.1" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="185" data-noteup-count-display="185"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="46.1" data-viibes-start="76" data-viibes-end="75"><A name="BK79"></A><B><a name="sec46.1subsec1" id="sec46_1subsec1"></A><a name="sec46.1" id="sec46_1"></A>46.1</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="46.1" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> If, in a civil proceeding in a court, the court finds that a party to the proceeding has infringed a right under Part I of another party to the proceeding, the court may make either of the following orders, or both:</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  An order directing the party who infringed the right to pay monetary compensation to the party whose right was infringed for loss arising out of the infringement, including compensation for injury to dignity, feelings and self-respect.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  An order directing the party who infringed the right to make restitution to the party whose right was infringed, other than through monetary compensation, for loss arising out of the infringement, including restitution for injury to dignity, feelings and self-respect.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 8</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec46.1subsec2" id="sec46_1subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="46.1" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Subsection (1) does not permit a person to commence an action based solely on an infringement of a right under Part I.  2006, c. 30, s. 8.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Penalty</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="46.2" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec46.2" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=46.2"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="46.2" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="3" data-noteup-count-display="3"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="46.2" data-viibes-start="77" data-viibes-end="76"><A name="BK80"></A><B><a name="sec46.2subsec1" id="sec46_2subsec1"></A><a name="sec46.2" id="sec46_2"></A>46.2</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="46.2" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Every person who contravenes <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="9" href="#sec9_smooth">section 9</A> or <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31" ss="14" href="#sec31subsec14_smooth">subsection 31 (14)</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="31.1" ss="8" href="#sec31.1subsec8_smooth">31.1 (8)</A> or <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="44" ss="13" href="#sec44subsec13_smooth">44 (13)</A> or an order of the Tribunal is guilty of an offence and on conviction is liable to a fine of not more than $25,000.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 8</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec46.2subsec2" id="sec46_2subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Consent to prosecution</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="46.2" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> No prosecution for an offence under this Act shall be instituted except with the consent in writing of the Attorney General.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 8</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Acts of officers, etc.</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="46.3" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec46.3" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=46.3"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="46.3" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="239" data-noteup-count-display="239"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="46.3" data-viibes-start="78" data-viibes-end="77"><A name="BK81"></A><B><a name="sec46.3subsec1" id="sec46_3subsec1"></A><a name="sec46.3" id="sec46_3"></A>46.3</B> <SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="46.3" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> For the purposes of this Act, except <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" ss="2" href="#sec2subsec2_smooth">subsection 2 (2)</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="5" ss="2" href="#sec5subsec2_smooth">subsection 5 (2)</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="7" href="#sec7_smooth">section 7</A> and <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="46.2" ss="1" href="#sec46.2subsec1_smooth">subsection 46.2 (1)</A>, any act or thing done or omitted to be done in the course of his or her employment by an officer, official, employee or agent of a corporation, trade union, trade or occupational association, unincorporated association or employers’ organization shall be deemed to be an act or thing done or omitted to be done by the corporation, trade union, trade or occupational association, unincorporated association or employers’ organization.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 8</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec46.3subsec2" id="sec46_3subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Opinion re authority or acquiescence</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="46.3" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> At the request of a corporation, trade union, trade or occupational association, unincorporated association or employers’ organization, the Tribunal in its decision shall make known whether or not, in its opinion, an act or thing done or omitted to be done by an officer, official, employee or agent was done or omitted to be done with or without the authority or acquiescence of the corporation, trade union, trade or occupational association, unincorporated association or employers’ organization, and the opinion does not affect the application of subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 8</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Act binds Crown</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="47" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec47" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=47"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="47" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="85" data-noteup-count-display="85"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="47" data-viibes-start="79" data-viibes-end="78"><A name="BK82"></A><B><a name="sec47subsec1" id="sec47subsec1"></A><a name="sec47" id="sec47"></A>47 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="47" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> This Act binds the Crown and every agency of the Crown.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 47 (1).</P></div>
 
<a name="sec47subsec2" id="sec47subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Act has primacy over other Acts</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="47" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Where a provision in an Act or regulation purports to require or authorize conduct that is a contravention of Part I, this Act applies and prevails unless the Act or regulation specifically provides that it is to apply despite this Act.  R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 47 (2).</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Regulations</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="48" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec48" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=48"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="48" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="4" data-noteup-count-display="4"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="48" data-viibes-start="80" data-viibes-end="79"><A name="BK83"></A><B><a name="sec48subsec1" id="sec48subsec1"></A><a name="sec48" id="sec48"></A>48 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="48" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council may make regulations,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  prescribing standards for assessing what is undue hardship for the purposes of <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="11" href="#sec11_smooth">section 11</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="17" href="#sec17_smooth">17</A> or<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="24" href="#sec24_smooth"> 24</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph"> (<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="1" href="#sec1_smooth">a.1</A>)  prescribing the manner in which income information, credit checks, credit references, rental history, guarantees or other similar business practices may be used by a landlord in selecting prospective tenants without infringing <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="2" href="#sec2_smooth">section 2</A>, and prescribing other similar business practices and the manner of their use, for the purposes of <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="21" ss="3" href="#sec21subsec3_smooth">subsection 21 (3)</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  prescribing matters for the purposes of <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="43" ss="3" href="#sec43subsec3_smooth">clause 43 (3)</A> (g);</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  respecting the Human Rights Legal Support Centre;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  governing any  matter that is necessary or advisable for the effective enforcement and administration of this Act.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  Repealed:  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 9 (1)</A>.</P>
 
<P class="footnote">R.S.O. 1990, c. H.19, s. 48; 1994, c. 27, s. 65 (25); 1997, c. 24, s. 212 (2); <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 9 (1)</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec48subsec2" id="sec48subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Human Rights Legal Support Centre</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="48" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> A regulation made under clause (1) (c) may,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  further define the Centre’s constitution, management and structure as set out in Part IV.1;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  prescribe powers and duties of the Centre and its members;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (c)  provide for limitations on the Centre’s powers under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.11" ss="4" href="#sec45.11subsec4_smooth">subsection 45.11 (4)</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (d)  prescribe services for the purposes of paragraph 3 of <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.13" ss="1" href="#sec45.13subsec1_smooth">subsection 45.13 (1)</A>;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (e)  further define the nature and scope of support services referred to in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.13" ss="1" href="#sec45.13subsec1_smooth">subsection 45.13 (1)</A>;</P>
