<P class="paragraph">  (f)  provide for factors to be considered in appointing members and specify the circumstances and manner in which they are to be considered; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (g)  provide for the term of appointment and reappointment of the Centre’s members;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (h)  Repealed: <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (3).</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (i)  provide for reporting requirements in addition to the annual report; </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (j)  provide for personal information to be collected by or on behalf of the Centre other than directly from the individual to whom the information relates, and for the manner in which the information is collected;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (k)  provide for the transfer from specified persons or entities of information, including personal information, that is relevant to carrying out the functions of the Centre;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (l)  provide for rules governing the confidentiality and security of information, including personal information, the collection, use and disclosure of such information, the retention and disposal of such information, and access to and correction of such information, including restrictions on any of these things, for the purposes of the carrying out of the functions of the Centre;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (m)  specify requirements and conditions for the funding of the Centre and for the Centre’s budget;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (n)  provide for audits of the statements and records of the Centre;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (o)  determine whether or not the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="42-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-b16/latest/rso-1990-c-b16.html">Business Corporations Act</A></I>, the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="84-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-c39/latest/rso-1990-c-c39.html">Corporations Information Act</A></I>
or the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="34647-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/so-2010-c-15/latest/so-2010-c-15.html">Not-for-Profit Corporations Act, 2010</A></I> or any provisions of those Acts apply to the Centre;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (p)  provide for anything necessary or advisable for the purposes of Part IV.1.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 9 (2)</A>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96992-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-20/latest/so-2017-c-20.html">2017, c. 20</A>, Sched. 8, <SPAN class="reflex2-link" link-count="1" link1="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-20/latest/so-2017-c-20.html#sec89" title1="Cutting Unnecessary Red Tape Act, 2017, SO 2017, c 20 (Ontario)" concatenated-id="96992" s="89" data-link-type="weak">s. 89</SPAN>; <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="97006-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2017-c-34/latest/so-2017-c-34.html">2017, c. 34</A>, Sched. 46, s. 20 (3).</P>
 

 
<A name="part_vi_transitional_provisions_109629"></A><P class="partnum"><A name="BK84"></A>part vi <BR>  transitional provisions</P>
 
<P class="headnote">Definitions</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="49" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec49" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=49"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="49" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="49" data-viibes-start="81" data-viibes-end="80"><A name="BK85"></A><B><a name="sec49" id="sec49"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="49" subsection="null" alinea="null">49</SPAN> </B>In this Part,</P></div>
 
<P class="definition">“effective date” means the day <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="4" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec4_smooth">sections 4</A> and<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="5" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec5_smooth"> 5</A> of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">Human Rights Code Amendment Act, 2006</A></I> come into force; (“date d’effet”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“new Part IV” means Part IV as it reads on and after the effective date; (“nouvelle partie IV”)</P>
 
<P class="definition">“old Part IV” means Part IV as it reads before the effective date. (“ancienne partie IV”)  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Orders respecting special programs</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="50" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec50" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=50"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="50" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-pen-to-square"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="50" data-viibes-start="82" data-viibes-end="81"><A name="BK86"></A><B><a name="sec50" id="sec50"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="50" subsection="null" alinea="null">50</SPAN> </B>On the fifth anniversary of the effective date, all orders that were made by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="14" ss="2" href="#sec14subsec2_smooth">subsection 14 (2)</A> before the effective date shall be null and void.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Application of <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" ss="3" href="#sec32subsec3_smooth">s. 32 (3)</A></P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="51" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec51" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=51"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="51" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="3" data-noteup-count-display="3"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="51" data-viibes-start="83" data-viibes-end="82"><A name="BK87"></A><B><a name="sec51" id="sec51"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="51" subsection="null" alinea="null">51</SPAN> </B>Subsection 32 (3) applies to the selection and appointment of persons to the Tribunal on or after the day <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="10" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec10_smooth">section 10</A> of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">Human Rights Code Amendment Act, 2006</A></I> comes into force.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Tribunal powers before effective date</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="52" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec52" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=52"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="52" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1" data-noteup-count-display="1"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="52" data-viibes-start="84" data-viibes-end="83"><A name="BK88"></A><B><a name="sec52subsec1" id="sec52subsec1"></A><a name="sec52" id="sec52"></A>52 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="52" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Despite anything to the contrary in the old Part IV, the Tribunal may, before the effective date,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  make rules in accordance with the new Part IV, including rules with respect to the reconsideration of Tribunal decisions; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  when dealing with complaints that are referred to it under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="36" href="#sec36_smooth">section 36</A> of the old Part IV, </P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (i)  deal with the complaint in accordance with the practices and procedures set out in the rules made under clause (a), </P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (ii)  exercise the powers described in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="39" href="#sec39_smooth">section 39</A> of the new Part IV, and</P>
 
<P class="subclause">  (iii)  dispose of the complaint in accordance with <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="40" href="#sec40_smooth">section 40</A> of the new Part IV.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec52subsec2" id="sec52subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Application </P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="52" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="41" href="#sec41_smooth">Sections 41</A> and<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="42" href="#sec42_smooth"> 42</A> of the new Part IV apply to rules made under clause (1) (a).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec52subsec3" id="sec52subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Tribunal decisions made before effective date</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="52" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Despite anything in the old Part IV, the following applies before the effective date with respect to a complaint that is referred to the Tribunal by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="36" href="#sec36_smooth">section 36</A> of the old Part IV on or after the day <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="10" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec10_smooth">section 10</A> of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">Human Rights Code Amendment Act, 2006</A></I> comes into force:</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  1.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="42" href="#sec42_smooth">Section 42</A> of the old Part IV does not apply to a decision of the Tribunal made with respect to the complaint.</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  2.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.7" href="#sec45.7_smooth">Sections 45.7</A> and <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.8" href="#sec45.8_smooth">45.8</A> of the new Part IV apply to a decision of the Tribunal made with respect to the complaint.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Complaints before Commission on effective date</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="53" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec53" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=53"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="53" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="204" data-noteup-count-display="204"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="53" data-viibes-start="85" data-viibes-end="84"><A name="BK89"></A><B><a name="sec53subsec1" id="sec53subsec1"></A><a name="sec53" id="sec53"></A>53 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="53" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> This section applies to a complaint filed with the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" ss="1" href="#sec32subsec1_smooth">subsection 32 (1)</A> of the old Part IV or initiated by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" ss="2" href="#sec32subsec2_smooth">subsection 32 (2)</A> of the old Part IV before the effective date.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec53subsec2" id="sec53subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Commission powers continued for six months</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Subject to subsection (3) and despite the repeal of the old Part IV, during the six-month period that begins on the effective date, the Commission shall continue to deal with complaints referred to in subsection (1) in accordance with <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" ss="3" href="#sec32subsec3_smooth">subsection 32 (3)</A> and <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="33" href="#sec33_smooth">sections 33</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">34</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="36" href="#sec36_smooth">36</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="37" href="#sec37_smooth">37</A> and<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="43" href="#sec43_smooth"> 43</A> of the old Part IV and, for that purpose, </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  the Commission has all the powers described in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" ss="3" href="#sec32subsec3_smooth">subsection 32 (3)</A> and <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="33" href="#sec33_smooth">sections 33</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="34" href="#sec34_smooth">34</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="36" href="#sec36_smooth">36</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="37" href="#sec37_smooth">37</A> and<A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="43" href="#sec43_smooth"> 43</A> of the old Part IV; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  the provisions referred to in clause (a) continue to apply with respect to the complaints, with necessary modifications.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec53subsec3" id="sec53subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Applications to Tribunal during six-month period</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> Subject to subsection (4), at any time during the six-month period referred to in subsection (2), the person who made a complaint that is continued under that subsection may, in accordance with the Tribunal rules, elect to abandon the complaint and make an application to the Tribunal with respect to the subject-matter of the complaint.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec53subsec4" id="sec53subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Expedited process</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The Tribunal shall make rules with respect to the practices and procedures that apply to an application under subsection (3) in order to ensure that the applications are dealt with in an expeditious manner.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec53subsec5" id="sec53subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Applications to Tribunal after six-month period</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> If, after the end of the six-month period referred to in subsection (2), the Commission has failed to deal with the merits of a complaint continued under that subsection and the complaint has not been withdrawn or settled, the complainant may make an application to the Tribunal with respect to the subject-matter of the complaint within a further six-month period after the end of the earlier six-month period.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec53subsec6" id="sec53subsec6"></A><P class="headnote">New Part IV applies</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="6" alinea="null">(6)</SPAN> The new Part IV applies to an application made under subsections (3) and (5).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec53subsec7" id="sec53subsec7"></A><P class="headnote">Disclosure of information</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="7" alinea="null">(7)</SPAN> Despite anything in the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="169-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-f31/latest/rso-1990-c-f31.html">Freedom of Information and Protection of Privacy Act</A></I>, at the request of a party to an application under subsection (3) or (5), the Commission may disclose to the party any information obtained by the Commission in the course of an investigation.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec53subsec8" id="sec53subsec8"></A><P class="headnote">Application barred</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="53" subsection="8" alinea="null">(8)</SPAN> No application, other than an application under subsection (3) or (5), may be made to the Tribunal if the subject-matter of the application is the same or substantially the same as the subject-matter of a complaint that was filed with the Commission under the old Part IV.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Settlements effected by Commission</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="54" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec54" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=54"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="54" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="7" data-noteup-count-display="7"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="54" data-viibes-start="86" data-viibes-end="85"><A name="BK90"></A><B><a name="sec54" id="sec54"></A><SPAN class="canlii_section" section="54" subsection="null" alinea="null">54</SPAN> </B><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="45.9" href="#sec45.9_smooth">Section 45.9</A> of the new Part IV applies to the enforcement of a settlement that,</P></div>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  was effected by the Commission under the old Part IV before the effective date or during the six-month period referred to in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="53" ss="2" href="#sec53subsec2_smooth">subsection 53 (2)</A>; and </P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  was agreed to in writing, signed by the parties and approved by the Commission.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Where complaints referred to Tribunal </P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="55" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec55" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=55"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="55" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="3" data-noteup-count-display="3"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="55" data-viibes-start="87" data-viibes-end="86"><A name="BK91"></A><B><a name="sec55subsec1" id="sec55subsec1"></A><a name="sec55" id="sec55"></A>55 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="55" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> This section applies to complaints that are referred to the Tribunal by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="36" href="#sec36_smooth">section 36</A> of the old Part IV before the effective date or during the six-month period referred to in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="53" ss="2" href="#sec53subsec2_smooth">subsection 53 (2)</A>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec55subsec2" id="sec55subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">New Part IV applies</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="55" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> On and after the effective date, the new Part IV applies to a complaint described in subsection (1) as though it were an application made to the Tribunal under that Part and the Tribunal shall deal with the complaint in accordance with the new Part IV.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec55subsec3" id="sec55subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Parties</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="55" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The Commission,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  shall continue to be a party to a complaint that was referred to the Tribunal before the effective date; and</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  subject to subsection (4), shall not be a party to a complaint referred to the Tribunal during the six-month period referred to in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="53" ss="2" href="#sec53subsec2_smooth">subsection 53 (2)</A>.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec55subsec4" id="sec55subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Same, exceptions</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="55" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> The Commission shall continue as a party to a complaint that was referred to the Tribunal during the six-month period referred to in <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="53" ss="2" href="#sec53subsec2_smooth">subsection 53 (2)</A> if,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  the complaint was initiated by the Commission under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="32" ss="2" href="#sec32subsec2_smooth">subsection 32 (2)</A> of the old Part IV; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  the Tribunal sets a date for the parties to appear before the Tribunal before the end of the six-month period.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec55subsec5" id="sec55subsec5"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="55" subsection="5" alinea="null">(5)</SPAN> Nothing in subsection (3) shall prevent,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  the Tribunal from adding the Commission as a party to a proceeding under <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="202-current-1" s="36" href="#sec36_smooth">section 36</A> of the new Part IV; or</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  the Commission from intervening in a proceeding with respect to a complaint described in subsection (1).  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Regulations, transitional matters</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="56" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec56" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=56"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="56" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="2" data-noteup-count-display="2"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="56" data-viibes-start="88" data-viibes-end="87"><A name="BK92"></A><B><a name="sec56subsec1" id="sec56subsec1"></A><a name="sec56" id="sec56"></A>56 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="56" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> The Lieutenant Governor in Council may make regulations providing for transitional matters which, in the opinion of the Lieutenant Governor in Council, are necessary or desirable to facilitate the implementation of the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">Human Rights Code Amendment Act, 2006</A></I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">.  2006, c. 30</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="10" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec10_smooth">s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec56subsec2" id="sec56subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="56" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> Without limiting the generality of subsection (1), the Lieutenant Governor in Council may make regulations,</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (a)  providing for transitional matters relating to the changes to the administration and functions of the Commission;</P>
 
<P class="paragraph">  (b)  dealing with any problems or issues arising as a result of the repeal or enactment of a provision of this Act by the <I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">Human Rights Code Amendment Act, 2006</A></I><A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">.  2006, c. 30</A>, <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" s="10" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html#sec10_smooth">s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec56subsec3" id="sec56subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Same</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="56" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> A regulation under this section may be general or specific in its application.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec56subsec4" id="sec56subsec4"></A><P class="headnote">Conflicts</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="56" subsection="4" alinea="null">(4)</SPAN> If there is a conflict between a provision in a regulation under this section and any provision of this Act or of any other regulation made under this Act, the regulation under this section prevails.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="headnote">Review</P>
 
<div class="paragWrapper" data-lbh-p-number="57" data-lbh-p-anchor="sec57" data-lbh-p-noteup-link="/en/#search/origin1=/en/on/laws/stat/rso-1990-c-h19/latest/rso-1990-c-h19.html&linkedNoteup=&section1=57"><div class="bootstrap unselectable viibes-marker-toolbox lbh-p-tools" data-with-parag="57" title="Paragraph tools"><div class="dropdown dropleft"><i data-toggle="dropdown" class="fa-thin fa-message-pen" data-noteup-count="1" data-noteup-count-display="1"></i><div class="dropdown-menu lbh-p-tools-menu"></div></div></div><P class="section" data-viibes-parag="57" data-viibes-start="89" data-viibes-end="88"><A name="BK93"></A><B><a name="sec57subsec1" id="sec57subsec1"></A><a name="sec57" id="sec57"></A>57 </B><SPAN class="canlii_section_with_subsection" section="57" subsection="1" alinea="null">(1)</SPAN> Three years after the effective date, the Minister shall appoint a person who shall undertake a review of the implementation and effectiveness of the changes resulting from the enactment of that Act.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P></div>
 
<a name="sec57subsec2" id="sec57subsec2"></A><P class="headnote">Public consultations</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="57" subsection="2" alinea="null">(2)</SPAN> In conducting a review under this section, the person appointed under subsection (1) shall hold public consultations.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 
<a name="sec57subsec3" id="sec57subsec3"></A><P class="headnote">Report to Minister</P>
 
<P class="subsection"><SPAN class="canlii_subsection" section="57" subsection="3" alinea="null">(3)</SPAN> The person appointed under subsection (1) shall prepare a report on his or her findings and submit the report to the Minister within one year of his or her appointment.  <A class="reflex2-link" concatenated-id="96723-current-1" href="/en/on/laws/astat/so-2006-c-30/latest/so-2006-c-30.html">2006, c. 30, s. 10</A>.</P>
 

 
<P class="line">______________</P>
 
<P class="line"> </P>

let citedByUrl = "/legislationTabs/citedBy/count/?legislationId=202&lang=en";

$.get(citedByUrl, function(data) {
	$("#citedBy-spinner").hide("fast");
	$("#citedBy-count").html("(" + data + ")");
})
.fail(function(jqXHR) {
	console.error(jqXHR);
})
.always(function() {
	$("#citedBy-spinner").hide("fast");
});

// load noteup counts only when the tab is selected
var loadedCitedBy = false;
$('a#noteup-tab').on('shown.bs.tab', function (e) {
	if (loadedCitedBy == false) {
		$.get("/legislationTabs/citedBy/content/?legislationId=202&lang=en", function(data) {
			$("#noteupContent").html(data);
			$("#noteup-spinner").hide("fast");
		})
		.fail(function(jqXHR) {
			console.error(jqXHR);
			$("#noteupContent").html("<p>An error occured while loading this tab.</p>");
		})
		.always(function() {
			$("#noteup-spinner").hide("fast");
		});
		
		loadedCitedBy = true;
	}
});

CanliiAnalytics.initDocumentEvents();
